*& Report  /SDF/HDB_SIZING // ZNEWHDB_SIZE
*&
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Estimates the memory requirement in HANA of non-HANA databases      *
*& When run on HANA, size the database using real memory consumption
*& values.
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*

REPORT /SDF/HDB_SIZING LINE-SIZE 101 LINE-COUNT 90 NO STANDARD PAGE HEADING.
CONSTANTS l_version TYPE c LENGTH 6 VALUE '99'.
TYPE-POOLS: abap. "700 compatibility

PARAMETERS p_dump TYPE i DEFAULT 20 MODIF ID prf.

AT SELECTION-SCREEN.
  IF sy-ucomm = 'CAL' AND sy-dbsys(3) = 'HDB'.
    p_calib  = abap_true.
    p_topobj = 50.
    p_mac    = abap_true.
    p_load   = abap_true.
    p_empt   = abap_true.
    CLEAR: prec_hi, prec_low.
    prec_med = abap_true.
    CLEAR p_slog.
    p_soh = abap_true.
  ENDIF.
  IF sy-ucomm = 'DB' OR sy-ucomm = 'CAL'.
    p_db = abap_true.
  ENDIF.
  IF sy-ucomm = 'FUL'.
    p_ful = abap_true.
  ENDIF.
  IF sy-ucomm = 'PRF'.
    p_prf = abap_true.
  ENDIF.

AT SELECTION-SCREEN OUTPUT.

  PERFORM check_table_existence USING 'ACDOCA' CHANGING exists.
  IF exists = abap_true.
    in_sfin = abap_true.
  ENDIF.

  PERFORM check_table_existence USING 'MATDOC' CHANGING exists.
  IF exists = abap_true.
    in_slog = abap_true.
  ENDIF.

  "grey out if not relevant
  IF p_ocpu = abap_true OR p_disp = abap_true.
    LOOP AT SCREEN.
      IF    screen-name <> 'P_GUID'
        AND screen-name <> 'P_GUID_C'
        AND screen-name <> 'P_OCPU'
        AND screen-name <> 'P_DISP'
        AND screen-name <> 'P_NORM'
        AND screen-name <> 'P_TOPOBJ'.
        screen-input = 0.
        MODIFY SCREEN.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.
  ENDIF.
  "make invisible if not relevant.
  LOOP AT SCREEN.
    IF sy-dbsys(3) <> 'HDB' AND screen-group1 = 'HDB'
      OR sy-dbsys(3) <> 'ORA' AND screen-group1 = 'STA'
      OR p_calib <> abap_true AND screen-group1 = 'CAL'
      OR p_ful <> abap_true AND screen-group1 = 'FUL'
      OR sy-dbsys(3) = 'HDB' AND p_calib <> abap_true AND screen-group1 = 'ANY'
      OR p_db <> abap_true AND screen-group1 = 'DB'
      OR p_prf <> abap_true AND screen-group1 = 'PRF'
      OR in_slog = abap_true AND screen-group1 = 'LOG'
      OR screen-group1 = 'FIN'. "always invisible
      screen-active = '0'.
      MODIFY SCREEN.
    ENDIF.
    IF screen-name = 'P_DISP'.
      CALL FUNCTION 'OM_FUNC_MODULE_EXIST'
        EXPORTING
          function_module = '/SDF/READ_HDB_SIZING_RESULTS_X'
        EXCEPTIONS
          not_existent    = 1
          OTHERS          = 2.
      IF sy-subrc IS NOT INITIAL.
        screen-active = '0'.
        MODIFY SCREEN.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.

    IF screen-name = 'P_GUID' OR screen-name = 'P_GUID_C'.
      CALL FUNCTION 'OM_FUNC_MODULE_EXIST'
        EXPORTING
          function_module = '/SDF/READ_HDB_SIZING_RESULTS_X'
        EXCEPTIONS
          not_existent    = 1
          OTHERS          = 2.
      IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
        IF p_ocpu = abap_true OR p_disp = abap_true.
          screen-input = '1'.
          MODIFY SCREEN.
        ELSE.
          screen-input = '0'.
          MODIFY SCREEN.
          CLEAR p_guid.
        ENDIF.
      ELSE.
        screen-active = '0'.
        MODIFY SCREEN.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.
    IF p_forc = abap_false AND ( screen-name = 'P_MREC' OR screen-name = 'P_SAGE' ).
      screen-input = '0'.
      MODIFY SCREEN.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.

  " Macros
  DEFINE b2gb.
    &1 = &1 / 1024 / 1024 / 1024.
  END-OF-DEFINITION.

  DEFINE k2gb.
    &1 = &1 / 1024 / 1024.
  END-OF-DEFINITION.

  DEFINE mb2b.
    &1 = &1 * 1024 * 1024.
  END-OF-DEFINITION.

  DEFINE mc_topheader.
    IF gt_top[] IS NOT INITIAL.
      WRITE /.
      WRITE / c_line.
      WRITE: / '|', AT 3  &1, AT 32 &3 CENTERED, AT 63 &5 CENTERED, AT 80 '|'.
      WRITE: / '|', AT 4  &2, AT 31 &4 CENTERED, AT 62 &6 CENTERED, AT 80 '|'.
      WRITE / c_line.
    ENDIF.
  END-OF-DEFINITION.

  DEFINE mc_sp. "2 columns inside a table
    IF &2 IS NOT INITIAL.
      WRITE: / '|', AT 3 &1, AT 61(18) &2 RIGHT-JUSTIFIED, AT 80 '|'.  "#EC NOTEXT
    ENDIF.
  END-OF-DEFINITION.

  DEFINE mc_spn. "2 columns inside a table for numeric
    IF &2 IS NOT INITIAL.
      WRITE: / '|', AT 3 &1, AT 63(17) &2 RIGHT-JUSTIFIED, AT 80 '|'.  "#EC NOTEXT
    ENDIF.
  END-OF-DEFINITION.

  DEFINE mc_sp1. " 1 column inside a table.
    IF &2 IS NOT INITIAL.
      MOVE &2 TO outln2.
      CONDENSE outln2.
      CONCATENATE &1 '(Total:' outln2 INTO outln2 SEPARATED BY space. "#EC NOTEXT
      CONCATENATE outln2 'GB)' INTO outln2.                "#EC NOTEXT
      WRITE: / '|', AT 3 outln2, AT 80 '|'.
    ENDIF.
  END-OF-DEFINITION.

  DEFINE mc_spi. "2 columns inside a table indented
    IF &2 IS NOT INITIAL.
      WRITE: / '|', AT 7 &1, AT 62(17) &2 RIGHT-JUSTIFIED, AT 80 '|'. "#EC NOTEXT
    ENDIF.
  END-OF-DEFINITION.

  DEFINE mc_s. "2 columns, no table
    IF &2 IS NOT INITIAL.
      WRITE: / '', AT 2 &1, AT 60(19) &2 RIGHT-JUSTIFIED.   "#EC NOTEXT
    ENDIF.
  END-OF-DEFINITION.

  DEFINE mc_sn. "2 columns, no table with numeric
    IF &2 IS NOT INITIAL.
      WRITE: / '', AT 2 &1, AT 63(17) &2 RIGHT-JUSTIFIED.   "#EC NOTEXT
    ENDIF.
  END-OF-DEFINITION.

  DEFINE mc_sp_t."1 column inside a table
    WRITE: / '|', AT 3(77) &1, AT 80 '|'.                   "#EC NOTEXT
  END-OF-DEFINITION.

  DEFINE mc_t2. "2 columns inside a table. Bigger 2nd table
    WRITE: / '|', AT 3 &1, AT 55(24) &2 RIGHT-JUSTIFIED, AT 80 '|'. "#EC NOTEXT
  END-OF-DEFINITION.

  DEFINE mc_sep_line. " Write a separator line inside a table.
    WRITE: / '|', AT 5 '-------------------------------------------------------------------------', AT 80 '|'.
  END-OF-DEFINITION.

  DEFINE mc_per. " CPU sizing details
    READ TABLE gt_cpu_per WITH KEY per = &1 ASSIGNING <cpu_per>.
    IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
      WRITE: / '|', AT 3 &2, AT 56(10) <cpu_per>-firstdate, AT 67(1) '-', AT 69(10) <cpu_per>-lastdate, AT 80 '|'. "#EC NOTEXT
    ENDIF.
  END-OF-DEFINITION.

  GET TIME STAMP FIELD startstamp.

  "It is not allowed to run the sizing report in Cloud system
  TRY.
      CALL METHOD (cos_util_class)=>is_cloud
        EXPORTING
          rv_is_cloud = is_cloud.
      IF is_cloud = abap_true.
        RETURN.
      ENDIF.
    CATCH cx_root.                                      "#EC NO_HANDLER
  ENDTRY.

  IF p_guid IS NOT INITIAL.
    p_guid_c = p_guid.
  ENDIF.
  IF p_guid_c IS NOT INITIAL.
    p_guid = p_guid_c.
  ENDIF.

  "Display-only choices
  IF p_disp = abap_true OR p_ocpu = abap_true.
    PERFORM read_selected_sizing USING p_guid.
    IF p_ocpu = abap_true.
      PERFORM sizing_calculation_cpu USING cpu_err.
    ENDIF.
    PERFORM b2gb_subtotals.
    PERFORM call_output USING 'OUTPUT_ON_SCREEN'.
    MESSAGE 'Sizing completed.' TYPE 'S'.                   "#EC NOTEXT
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  "Find out what needs to be sized
  do_soh = p_soh.
  do_s4 = p_slog. "p_slog cannot be renamed

  "Is persistent memory used
  IF sy-dbsys(3) = 'HDB'.
    TRY.
      EXEC SQL.
        SELECT 'X' AS is_pers_mem INTO :is_pers_mem FROM sys.m_monitors WHERE view_name = 'M_PERSISTENT_MEMORY_VOLUMES'
      ENDEXEC.                                          "#EC CI_EXECSQL
      IF is_pers_mem = abap_true.
        EXEC SQL.
          SELECT CASE WHEN count(1) = 0 THEN '' ELSE 'X' END AS is_pers_mem INTO :is_pers_mem
            FROM PUBLIC.M_PERSISTENT_MEMORY_VOLUMES
            WHERE is_direct_access_supported = 'true'
              AND port IN ( SELECT DISTINCT port FROM SYS.M_SERVICES WHERE service_name = 'indexserver' )
        ENDEXEC.                                        "#EC CI_EXECSQL
      ENDIF.
      wa_techd-is_pers_mem = is_pers_mem.
    CATCH cx_sy_native_sql_error.
      wa_techd-is_pers_mem = abap_false.
    ENDTRY.
  ENDIF.

  IF do_s4 = abap_true.
    PERFORM check_table_existence USING 'BSIS' CHANGING exists.
    IF exists = abap_true AND in_sfin = abap_false.
      do_sfin = abap_true.
    ENDIF.

    PERFORM check_table_existence USING 'VBAK' CHANGING exists.
    IF exists = abap_true AND in_slog = abap_false.
      do_slog = abap_true.
    ENDIF.

    PERFORM check_table_existence USING 'MLDOC' CHANGING exists.
    IF exists = abap_true.
      in_sml = abap_true.
    ELSEIF in_sfin = abap_true OR do_sfin = abap_true.
      do_sml = abap_true.
    ENDIF.
  ENDIF.

  "Only HANA 2.0 supported.
  p_hdb2 = abap_true.
  CLEAR p_hdb1.
  p_mshl = abap_true.
  udiv_default = 43696. "bytes

  "Overwrites (hidden) screen selection for SAP_BASIS version.
  IF do_soh = abap_true.
    "no 753 with SoH
    CLEAR p_bas2.
    p_bas1 = abap_true.
    p_lraw = 5000. "bytes
  ELSE.
    "if S/4, we size only for >=1809. Therefore 753.
    CLEAR p_bas1.
    p_bas2 = abap_true.
    p_lraw = 1000. "bytes
  ENDIF.

  "Check choice of technical options
  IF p_paral < 1.
    MESSAGE e090(sada) WITH 'Unacceptable value for parallel degree:' p_paral
                            'Please enter value bigger than 0.'. "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.

  IF prec_low = abap_true.
    wa_techd-prec = 'L'.
  ELSEIF prec_hi = abap_true.
    wa_techd-prec = 'H'.
  ELSE.
    wa_techd-prec = 'M'.
  ENDIF.
  bucket_size = p_buk.
  max_dump    = p_dump.
  taana_min_date = sy-datum - p_taan.

  CALL FUNCTION 'SPBT_INITIALIZE'
    EXPORTING
      group_name                     = p_group
    IMPORTING
      free_pbt_wps                   = maxrfc
    EXCEPTIONS
      invalid_group_name             = 1
      internal_error                 = 2
      pbt_env_already_initialized    = 3
      currently_no_resources_avail   = 4
      no_pbt_resources_found         = 5
      cant_init_different_pbt_groups = 6
      OTHERS                         = 7.

  CASE sy-subrc.
    WHEN 0.
      IF p_paral >= maxrfc.
        p_paral = maxrfc - 2.
        IF p_paral < 1.
          p_paral = 1.
        ENDIF.
      ENDIF.
    WHEN 1.
      MESSAGE e090(sada) WITH 'Server group' p_group 'is invalid.'. "#EC NOTEXT
    WHEN 4.
      MESSAGE e090(sada) WITH 'There are currently no' 'available resources on server group' p_group '.'. "#EC NOTEXT
    WHEN OTHERS.
      MESSAGE e090(sada) WITH 'An error occurred with server group' p_group '.'. "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDCASE.

  " Check authority
  AUTHORITY-CHECK OBJECT 'S_ADMI_FCD' ID 'S_ADMI_FCD' FIELD 'PADM'.
  IF sy-subrc IS NOT INITIAL.
    MESSAGE 'You do not have the authorization to run this report. Refer to the FAQ of Note 1872170.' TYPE 'E'. "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.

  "Check job name - Relevant for Readiness Check
  CALL FUNCTION 'GET_JOB_RUNTIME_INFO'
    IMPORTING
      jobname         = jobname
      jobcount        = jobcount
    EXCEPTIONS
      no_runtime_info = 1
      OTHERS          = 2.

  "Check installation (Z report)
  CASE sy-repid.
    WHEN 'ZNEWHDB_SIZE'.
      funcname = 'Z_COLLECT_STATS'.
      PERFORM check_install.
    WHEN '/SDF/HDB_SIZING'.
      funcname = '/SDF/COLLECT_DB_STATS'.
    WHEN OTHERS.
      funcname = 'Z_COLLECT_STATS'.
  ENDCASE.

  "Start work
  "If Global temp tables exist, exclude them
  IF sy-dbsys(3) <> 'HDB'.
    CALL FUNCTION 'DDIF_NAMETAB_GET'
      EXPORTING
        tabname    = 'DD02L'
        lfieldname = 'IS_GTT'
      EXCEPTIONS
        not_found  = 1
        OTHERS     = 2.
    IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
      where_clause = 'IS_GTT = SPACE'.                      "#EC NOTEXT
    ENDIF.
  ENDIF.

  "Collect all tables selected for sizing
  SELECT * FROM dd02l INTO gs_dd02l
    WHERE as4local = 'A' AND tabname IN so_tab AND tabclass IN ('TRANSP', 'CLUSTER' , 'POOL') AND (where_clause).
    table_item-table_name = gs_dd02l-tabname.
    table_item-tab_type   = gs_dd02l-tabclass.
    table_item-db_table   = gs_dd02l-sqltab.
    IF table_item-db_table IS INITIAL.
      table_item-db_table = table_item-table_name.
    ENDIF.
    APPEND table_item TO gt_input.
  ENDSELECT.
  CLEAR table_item.
  SORT gt_input BY table_name.

  IF gt_input IS INITIAL.
    RETURN. "no valid tables in selection.
  ENDIF.

  SORT gt_input BY db_table.

  " identify multiplex tables and adapt their db name.
  IF gt_input IS NOT INITIAL.
    SELECT tabname FROM dd02l INTO TABLE tt_t_multi FOR ALL ENTRIES IN gt_input
      WHERE as4local = 'A' AND tabclass = 'VIEW' AND tabname = gt_input-db_table.
    LOOP AT tt_t_multi INTO ls_tablename.
      READ TABLE gt_input ASSIGNING <item> WITH KEY db_table = ls_tablename BINARY SEARCH.
      IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
        <item>-db_table = <item>-table_name. "keep sort.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.
    CLEAR: tt_t_multi[], ls_tablename.
  ENDIF.

  IF p_calib = abap_true.
    mode = 'CAL'.
  ELSE.
    mode = 'NOR'.
  ENDIF.

  MESSAGE 'Start of statistics collection' TYPE 'S'.        "#EC NOTEXT
  PERFORM collect_stats USING mode.

  MESSAGE s090(sada) WITH 'Start of sizing calculation'.    "#EC NOTEXT
*
* All results now in gt_tables and gt_columns / gt_real*
*
  IF sy-dbsys(3) <> 'HDB' OR p_calib = abap_true.

    "Collect TAANA results if requested
    IF p_tago = abap_true.
      PERFORM read_taana.
    ENDIF.

    "Distinguish row and column store tables
    PERFORM fill_row_list. "Only use hardcoded list. Do not trust old DDIC
    LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item>.
      READ TABLE gt_row_tab WITH KEY table_line = <item>-table_name TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS BINARY SEARCH.
      IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL AND <item>-record_count < 500000000.
        <item>-store = 'RS'.
      ELSE.
        <item>-store = 'CS'.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.

    "Sort out tables with errors
    LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item>.
      IF <item>-return_code = 98.
        IF <item>-records_sampled >= 10000.
          "partial success
          CLEAR ls_partial.
          MOVE-CORRESPONDING <item> TO ls_partial.
          APPEND ls_partial TO gt_partial.
          CLEAR ls_partial.
        ELSE.
          MOVE-CORRESPONDING <item> TO ls_error.
          ls_error-return_code = -1.
          APPEND ls_error TO gt_error.
          CLEAR ls_error.
          DELETE gt_tables.
        ENDIF.
      ELSEIF <item>-record_count = -1 OR <item>-return_code <> 0.
        MOVE-CORRESPONDING <item> TO ls_error.
        ls_error-return_code = -1.
        APPEND ls_error TO gt_error.
        CLEAR ls_error.
        DELETE gt_tables.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.

* fill embedded tables.
    LOOP AT gt_columns ASSIGNING <columns>.
      READ TABLE gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WITH KEY table_name = <columns>-table_name BINARY SEARCH.
      IF <item>-store = 'CS'.
        MOVE-CORRESPONDING <columns> TO gs_cs_size.
        APPEND gs_cs_size TO <item>-cs_cols.
      ELSE.
        MOVE-CORRESPONDING <columns> TO gs_rs_size.
        APPEND gs_rs_size TO <item>-rs_cols.
      ENDIF.
      CLEAR: gs_cs_size, gs_rs_size.
    ENDLOOP.

    REFRESH gt_columns.
    PERFORM fill_indiv_indexes CHANGING gt_tables.
    PERFORM fill_nse_list CHANGING gt_nse_list.
    PERFORM sizing_calculation CHANGING gt_tables.

*start of calibration specific code.
    SORT gt_realcs      BY table_name column_name part_id.
    SORT gt_realrsindex BY table_name index_name.
    SORT gt_realrs      BY table_name.

    LOOP AT gt_realcs ASSIGNING <real_cs>.
      READ TABLE gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WITH KEY table_name = <real_cs>-table_name BINARY SEARCH.
      IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
        IF <item>-store = 'CS'.
          READ TABLE <item>-cs_cols ASSIGNING <cs_size> WITH KEY column_name = <real_cs>-column_name.
          IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
            <cs_size>-part_id  = <real_cs>-part_id.
            <cs_size>-ms_total = <cs_size>-ms_total + <real_cs>-ms_total.
            <cs_size>-ms_main  = <cs_size>-ms_main  + <real_cs>-ms_main.
            <cs_size>-distinct_count = <cs_size>-distinct_count + <real_cs>-distinct_count.
            " wrong if partitioned !
            <cs_size>-loaded           = <real_cs>-loaded.
            <cs_size>-index_loaded     = <real_cs>-index_loaded.
            <cs_size>-compression_type = <real_cs>-compression_type.
            <cs_size>-ms_dict  = <cs_size>-ms_dict  + <real_cs>-ms_dict.
            <cs_size>-ms_index = <cs_size>-ms_index + <real_cs>-ms_index.
            <cs_size>-ms_data  = <cs_size>-ms_data  + <real_cs>-ms_data.
            <cs_size>-ms_misc  = <cs_size>-ms_misc  + <real_cs>-ms_misc.
            <cs_size>-ms_hl    = <cs_size>-ms_hl    + <real_cs>-ms_hl.
          ELSE."non-unique from JE. Aging columns. ESH. FT.
            IF <item>-record_count > 0.
              FIND ALL OCCURRENCES OF '$' IN <real_cs>-column_name MATCH COUNT dollar_count.
              IF dollar_count > 2 OR <real_cs>-column_name(1)  = '_'
                                  OR <real_cs>-column_name(13) = '$_SYS_SHADOW_'
                                  OR <real_cs>-column_name(5)  = '$esh:'.
                CLEAR gs_cs_size.
                MOVE-CORRESPONDING <real_cs> TO gs_cs_size.
                APPEND gs_cs_size TO <item>-cs_cols.
              ELSE.
                WRITE: / 'Could not find column', <real_cs>-table_name, <real_cs>-column_name. "#EC NOTEXT
              ENDIF.
            ENDIF.
          ENDIF.
        ELSE.
          WRITE: / 'Table in RS, expected in CS', <real_cs>-table_name, <real_cs>-column_name. "#EC NOTEXT
        ENDIF.
      ELSE.
        WRITE: / 'Table not found in gt_tables', <real_cs>-table_name, <real_cs>-column_name. "#EC NOTEXT
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.

    LOOP AT gt_realrs ASSIGNING <real_rs>.
      READ TABLE gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WITH KEY table_name = <real_rs>-table_name BINARY SEARCH.
      IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
        IF <item>-store = 'RS'.
          CLEAR gs_rs_size.
          MOVE-CORRESPONDING <real_rs> TO gs_rs_size.
          APPEND gs_rs_size TO <item>-rs_cols.
        ELSE.
          WRITE: / 'Table in CS, expected in RS', <real_rs>-table_name. "#EC NOTEXT
        ENDIF.
      ELSE.
        WRITE: / 'Table not found in gt_tables', <real_rs>-table_name. "#EC NOTEXT
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.

    LOOP AT gt_realrsindex ASSIGNING <real_rsindex>.
      READ TABLE gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WITH KEY table_name = <real_rsindex>-table_name BINARY SEARCH.
      IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
        IF <item>-store = 'RS'.
          IF <real_rsindex>-index_name(13) = '_SYS_TREE_RS_'.
            READ TABLE <item>-rs_cols ASSIGNING <rs_size> WITH KEY column_name = <real_rsindex>-index_name(13).
            IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
              <rs_size>-fixed_size = <real_rsindex>-index_size.
            ELSE.
              WRITE: / <real_rsindex>-table_name, 'no RS PK sized. Table is maybe CS!?'.   "#EC NOTEXT
            ENDIF.
          ELSEIF <real_rsindex>-index_name CS '~0'
              OR <real_rsindex>-index_name CS '^0'.
            READ TABLE <item>-rs_cols ASSIGNING <rs_size> WITH KEY column_name = '_SYS_TREE_RS_'.
            IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
              <rs_size>-fixed_size = <real_rsindex>-index_size.
            ENDIF.
          ELSEIF <real_rsindex>-index_name CS '~'.
            READ TABLE <item>-rs_cols ASSIGNING <rs_size> WITH KEY column_name = <real_rsindex>-index_name.
            IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
              <rs_size>-fixed_size = <real_rsindex>-index_size.
            ENDIF.
          ELSE. "something else found  "should not happen
            WRITE: / <real_rsindex>-table_name, <real_rsindex>-index_name, 'found but not sized'."#EC NOTEXT
          ENDIF.
        ELSE.
          WRITE: / 'Table in CS, expected in RS', <item>-table_name. "#EC NOTEXT
        ENDIF.
      ELSE.
        WRITE: / 'Table not found in gt_tables', <item>-table_name. "#EC NOTEXT
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.
*end of calibration specific code.
  ELSE. "simple run on HANA
    LOOP AT gt_realcs ASSIGNING <real_cs>.
      CLEAR gs_cs_size.
      MOVE-CORRESPONDING <real_cs> TO gs_cs_size.
      READ TABLE gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WITH KEY table_name = <real_cs>-table_name BINARY SEARCH.
      IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
        <item>-store = 'CS'.
        "We assume no conversion to NSE on column level
        IF <real_cs>-load_unit IS NOT INITIAL AND <real_cs>-column_name(1) <> '$'.
          <item>-load_unit = <real_cs>-load_unit.
        ENDIF.
        APPEND gs_cs_size TO <item>-cs_cols.
        CLEAR gs_cs_size.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.

    LOOP AT gt_realrs ASSIGNING <real_rs>.
      CLEAR gs_rs_size.
      MOVE-CORRESPONDING <real_rs> TO gs_rs_size.
      READ TABLE gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WITH KEY table_name = <real_rs>-table_name BINARY SEARCH.
      IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
        <item>-store = 'RS'.
        APPEND gs_rs_size TO <item>-rs_cols.
        CLEAR gs_rs_size.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.

    LOOP AT gt_realrsindex ASSIGNING <real_rsindex>.
      CLEAR gs_rs_size.
      gs_rs_size-column_name = <real_rsindex>-index_name.
      gs_rs_size-fixed_size  = <real_rsindex>-index_size.
      READ TABLE gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WITH KEY table_name = <real_rsindex>-table_name BINARY SEARCH.
      IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
        APPEND gs_rs_size TO <item>-rs_cols.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.

    CLEAR: gt_realrs, gt_realcs, gt_realrsindex.
    DESCRIBE TABLE gt_tables LINES realsize_cnt.

    "idendify DDIC secondary keys.
    PERFORM fill_index_list.
    SORT gt_index BY sqltab fieldname position.

    LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WHERE store = 'CS'.
      LOOP AT <item>-cs_cols ASSIGNING <cs_size> WHERE column_name(1) = '$'.
        FIND ALL OCCURRENCES OF '$' IN <cs_size>-column_name MATCH COUNT dollar_count.
        IF dollar_count > 2.
          searchfield = <cs_size>-column_name.
          DO.
            SEARCH searchfield+1 FOR '$'.
            IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
              IF sy-fdpos = 0. "double $$
                sy-fdpos = 1.
              ENDIF.
              gs_nu_index-fieldname = searchfield+1(sy-fdpos).
              gs_nu_index-sqltab    = <item>-table_name.
              ADD 1 TO gs_nu_index-position.
              APPEND gs_nu_index TO gt_nu_index.
              fdpos = sy-fdpos + 1.
              searchfield = searchfield+fdpos.
            ELSE.
              CLEAR: gs_nu_index, searchfield.
              EXIT.
            ENDIF.
          ENDDO.
          DESCRIBE TABLE gt_nu_index LINES lv_maxpos.
          LOOP AT gt_nu_index ASSIGNING <nu_idx>.
            LOOP AT gt_index ASSIGNING <idx> WHERE sqltab    = <nu_idx>-sqltab
                                               AND fieldname = <nu_idx>-fieldname
                                               AND position  = <nu_idx>-position.
              IF <nu_idx>-position = '1'.
                MOVE-CORRESPONDING <idx> TO gs_posindex.
                APPEND gs_posindex TO gt_posindex.
              ELSE.
                lv_pos = <idx>-position - 1.
                LOOP AT gt_posindex ASSIGNING <po_idx>.
                  IF <po_idx>-indexname = <idx>-indexname AND <po_idx>-position = lv_pos.
                    ADD 1 TO <po_idx>-position.
                  ENDIF.
                ENDLOOP.
              ENDIF.
            ENDLOOP.
            IF gt_posindex IS INITIAL.
              EXIT.
            ENDIF.
          ENDLOOP.
          READ TABLE gt_posindex WITH KEY position = lv_maxpos TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS.
          IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
            <cs_size>-has_index = 'P'.
          ENDIF.
          CLEAR: gt_nu_index, gt_posindex, lv_pos, lv_maxpos.
        ENDIF.
      ENDLOOP.
    ENDLOOP.
  ENDIF.

  "Estimate move to row store and lraw LOB conversion
  IF do_slog = abap_true AND sy-dbsys(3) = 'HDB'.
    PERFORM changes_s4.
  ENDIF.

  PERFORM calculate_subtotals.
  PERFORM get_anydb_size CHANGING wa_techd-anydbsize_n
                                  wa_techd-anydbsizedate.
  PERFORM sizing_calculation_cpu USING cpu_err.
  PERFORM fill_tech_details.
  "Persist results.
  IF sy-batch = abap_true OR p_db = abap_true.
    PERFORM call_output USING 'WRITE_TO_DB'.
  ENDIF.
  "convert to GiB for display
  PERFORM b2gb_subtotals.

  "Check reliability
  IF est_init_data > 0 AND gt_error IS NOT INITIAL.
    PERFORM check_reliability USING gt_error est_init_data CHANGING error_ratio.
  ENDIF.

  " Write the output
  PERFORM call_output USING 'OUTPUT_ON_SCREEN'.

  IF p_calib = abap_true.
    WRITE: / 'Reality:',    'main', 'dict', 'data', 'index', 'misc'. "#EC NOTEXT
    WRITE: / 'Estimation:', 'main', 'dict', 'data', 'index', 'misc'. "#EC NOTEXT
    LOOP AT lt_cs_cal ASSIGNING <cscal>.
      WRITE: / <cscal>-column_name, <cscal>-ms_main,     <cscal>-ms_dict,     <cscal>-ms_data,     <cscal>-ms_index,     <cscal>-ms_misc.
      WRITE: / <cscal>-column_name, <cscal>-est_ms_main, <cscal>-est_ms_dict, <cscal>-est_ms_data, <cscal>-est_ms_index, <cscal>-est_ms_misc.
    ENDLOOP.
    WRITE /.
  ENDIF.

  MESSAGE 'End of sizing calculation' TYPE 'S'.             "#EC NOTEXT
  MESSAGE 'Sizing done. Check result in the spool request.' TYPE 'S'. "#EC NOTEXT

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& FORM  check_table_existence
*& Check whether a table exists.
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM check_table_existence USING    iv_table  TYPE tabname
                           CHANGING cv_exists TYPE abap_bool.
  DATA lv_subrc TYPE sysubrc.
  CALL FUNCTION 'DD_EXIST_TABLE'
    EXPORTING
      tabname      = iv_table
      status       = 'A'
    IMPORTING
      subrc        = lv_subrc
    EXCEPTIONS
      wrong_status = 1
      OTHERS       = 2.
  IF lv_subrc IS INITIAL AND sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
    cv_exists = abap_true.
  ELSE.
    cv_exists = abap_false.
  ENDIF.
ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& FORM  do_rfc
*& Call RFC to read stats
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*

FORM do_rfc TABLES gt_bucket TYPE ty_t_hana_db_size
            USING  bucket    TYPE ty_hana_db_size-bucket
                   prec      TYPE c
                   mode      TYPE string.

  EXPORT p1 = gt_bucket TO DATA BUFFER data.
  DO.
    IF mode(3) = '1ST'.
      taskname = bucket."convert to c
      CONCATENATE mode taskname INTO taskname.
    ELSE. " retry with only one db table.
      READ TABLE gt_bucket INTO table_item INDEX 1.
      CONCATENATE mode table_item-db_table INTO taskname.
    ENDIF.
    CALL FUNCTION funcname STARTING NEW TASK taskname DESTINATION IN GROUP p_group
      PERFORMING collect_all ON END OF TASK
      EXPORTING
        precision             = prec
        mode                  = mode
        load                  = p_load
        hl                    = p_hl
        mac                   = p_mac
        clustprec             = p_clus
        mshl                  = p_mshl
        daag                  = p_daag
        force_count           = p_forc
        stat_age              = p_sage
        min_rec_cnt           = p_mrec
        hdb_empty_tables      = p_empt
        lraw                  = p_lraw
      CHANGING
        data                  = data
      EXCEPTIONS
*        system_error          = 1
        system_failure        = 2
        communication_failure = 3
        resource_failure      = 4
        OTHERS                = 5.

    CASE sy-subrc.
      WHEN 0.
        ADD 1 TO l_sent.
        EXIT.
      WHEN 4.
        max_act = l_act - 1.
        WAIT UNTIL l_act < max_act. "wait for free wp
      WHEN OTHERS.
        MESSAGE x000(00).
    ENDCASE.
  ENDDO.
  l_act  = l_sent - l_recvd.

ENDFORM.                    "do_rfc

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& FORM  collect_all
*& Callback for RFC to collect results
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*

FORM collect_all                                            "#EC CALLED
  USING ret TYPE clike.                                     "#EC NEEDED

  DATA:
    data_part           TYPE xstring,
    lt_tables_part      TYPE ty_t_hana_db_size,
    lt_columns_part     TYPE TABLE OF ty_columns,
    lt_realrsindex_part TYPE typ_t_realrsindex,
    lt_realrs_part      TYPE typ_t_realrs,
    lt_realcs_part      TYPE typ_t_realcs,
    l_progress          TYPE p DECIMALS 1.

  RECEIVE RESULTS FROM FUNCTION funcname
    CHANGING
      data                    = data_part
      EXCEPTIONS
        system_error          = 1
        system_failure        = 2
        communication_failure = 3
        OTHERS                = 5.

  CASE sy-subrc.
    WHEN 0.
      IMPORT p1 = lt_tables_part
             p2 = lt_columns_part
             p3 = lt_realrsindex_part
             p4 = lt_realrs_part
             p5 = lt_realcs_part
             FROM DATA BUFFER data_part.
      APPEND LINES OF lt_tables_part TO gt_tables.
      APPEND LINES OF lt_columns_part TO gt_columns.
      APPEND LINES OF lt_realrsindex_part TO gt_realrsindex.
      APPEND LINES OF lt_realrs_part TO gt_realrs.
      APPEND LINES OF lt_realcs_part TO gt_realcs.
    WHEN 2.
      IF ret(3) = 'RET'. "this is a retry => Log error.
        LOOP AT gt_input INTO table_item WHERE db_table = ret+6.
          ls_error-table_name  = table_item-table_name.
          ls_error-return_code = 99.
          IF table_item-tab_type = 'POOL' AND sy-dbsys(3) = 'DB6'.
            ls_error-error_message = 'DB2 DBSL Error. Check FAQ document attached to SAP Note 1872170.'. "#EC NOTEXT
          ELSE.
            ls_error-error_message = 'Check ST22.'.          "#EC NOTEXT
          ENDIF.
          APPEND ls_error TO gt_error.
        ENDLOOP.
        MESSAGE s090(sada) WITH 'An error occurred while processing table' table_item-table_name
                                'Check ST22 for details.'.       "#EC NOTEXT

      ELSE. " this is the first time => retry.
        ADD 1 TO l_dump.
        MESSAGE 'An error occurred in RFC call. Check ST22 for details. The RFC call will be re-executed.' TYPE 'S'. "#EC NOTEXT
        IF l_dump > max_dump.
          " Too many RFC calls terminated in error. Check in ST22
          " the dumps that occurred before the MESSAGE_TYPE_X.
          " The MESSAGE_TYPE_X dump itself is not the problem.
          MESSAGE x000(00).
        ENDIF.
        LOOP AT gt_input INTO table_item WHERE bucket = ret+6.
          APPEND table_item TO lt_retry.
        ENDLOOP.
      ENDIF.
    WHEN OTHERS.
      MESSAGE x000(00).
  ENDCASE.
  ADD 1 TO l_recvd.
  l_act = l_sent - l_recvd.
  IF mode(3) = '1ST'.
    l_progress = l_recvd / nb_buckets * 100.
    MESSAGE s001(sada) WITH l_progress '% of statistics collection' 'is done.'. "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.
  IF mode(3) = 'RET'.
    l_progress = l_recvd / l_retrycnt * 100.
    MESSAGE s090(sada) WITH l_progress '% of reprocessing is done.'. "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.
ENDFORM.                    "collect_all

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& FORM  fill_row_list
*& Append list of Row Store tables (See SAP Note 1850112)
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*

FORM fill_row_list.
  DATA l_rsnotins4 TYPE abap_bool.
  DEFINE mc_rs.
    ls_tablename = &1.
    IF l_rsnotins4 = abap_false.
      "tables that will always be in RS
      APPEND ls_tablename TO gt_row_tab.
    ELSE.
      IF do_s4 = abap_false.
        "Table is in RS if SoH but CS in S4
        APPEND ls_tablename TO gt_row_tab.
      ELSE.
        "S4 sizing. Track tables that should not be in RS
        APPEND ls_tablename TO gt_rownots4_tab.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.
  END-OF-DEFINITION.

  "RS tables in 2022.
  mc_rs '/IWBEP/I_MGW_CTC'. mc_rs '/IWFND/I_MED_SRK'.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  check_install
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      Check the installation if Z version is correctly installed.
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*

FORM check_install.

  DATA:
    l_remoteflag  TYPE rs38l-remote,
    lt_exeplist   TYPE TABLE OF rsexc,
    lt_import     TYPE TABLE OF rsimp,
    lt_changing   TYPE TABLE OF rscha,
    lt_doku       TYPE TABLE OF funct,
    lt_export     TYPE TABLE OF rsexp,
    lt_tabparam   TYPE TABLE OF rstbl,
    lines         TYPE i,
    l_import_ko   TYPE boolean,
    l_changing_ko TYPE boolean,
    l_fixpt       TYPE progdir-fixpt.

  DEFINE mc_parchk.
    READ TABLE lt_import TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS
          WITH KEY parameter = &1
                   typ       = &2
                   optional  = abap_true.
    IF sy-subrc IS NOT INITIAL.
      l_import_ko = abap_true.
    ENDIF.
  END-OF-DEFINITION.

  SELECT SINGLE fixpt FROM progdir INTO l_fixpt WHERE name = sy-repid AND state = 'A'.

  IF sy-subrc IS NOT INITIAL.
    MESSAGE 'Report ZNEWHDBSIZE is not installed properly. No entry found in REPOSRC.' TYPE 'E'. "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.

  IF l_fixpt IS INITIAL.
    MESSAGE 'The Fixed point arithmetic flag must not be unticked. Tick the flag and execute the report once again.' TYPE 'E'. "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.
  CALL FUNCTION 'FUNCTION_IMPORT_DOKU'
    EXPORTING
      funcname           = funcname
    IMPORTING
      remote_call        = l_remoteflag
    TABLES
      dokumentation      = lt_doku
      export_parameter   = lt_export
      exception_list     = lt_exeplist
      import_parameter   = lt_import
      changing_parameter = lt_changing
      tables_parameter   = lt_tabparam
    EXCEPTIONS
      error_message      = 1
      function_not_found = 2
      invalid_name       = 3
      OTHERS             = 4.
  IF sy-subrc IS NOT INITIAL.
    MESSAGE 'Function module Z_COLLECT_STATS was not found. Check the installation instructions in SAP Note 1872170.' TYPE 'E'. "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.
  IF l_remoteflag IS INITIAL.
    MESSAGE 'The remote flag of Z_COLLECT_STATS is not set. Check the installation instructions in SAP Note 1872170.' TYPE 'E'. "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.
  IF lt_export IS NOT INITIAL.
    MESSAGE 'Function module Z_COLLECT_STATS has incorrect export parameters. Check the installation instructions in SAP Note 1872170.' TYPE 'E'. "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.

  DESCRIBE TABLE lt_import LINES lines.
  IF lines <> 13.
    l_import_ko = abap_true.
  ENDIF.

  mc_parchk 'PRECISION' 'DTPRECINT'.
  mc_parchk 'MODE' 'STRING'.
  mc_parchk 'LOAD' 'BOOLEAN'.
  mc_parchk 'HL' 'BOOLEAN'.
  mc_parchk 'MAC' 'BOOLEAN'.
  mc_parchk 'CLUSTPREC' 'DTPRECINT'.
  mc_parchk 'MSHL' 'BOOLEAN'.
  mc_parchk 'DAAG' 'NUMC3'.
  mc_parchk 'FORCE_COUNT' 'BOOLEAN'.
  mc_parchk 'STAT_AGE' 'INT4'.
  mc_parchk 'MIN_REC_CNT' 'INT4'.
  mc_parchk 'HDB_EMPTY_TABLES' 'BOOLEAN'.
  mc_parchk 'LRAW' 'INT4'.

  IF l_import_ko = abap_true.
    MESSAGE 'Function module Z_COLLECT_STATS has incorrect import parameters. Check the installation instructions in SAP Note 1872170.' TYPE 'E'. "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.
  DESCRIBE TABLE lt_changing LINES lines.
  IF lines <> 1.
    l_changing_ko = abap_true.
  ENDIF.
  READ TABLE lt_changing TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS WITH KEY parameter = 'DATA'
                                                         typ       = 'XSTRING'.
  IF sy-subrc IS NOT INITIAL.
    l_changing_ko = abap_true.
  ENDIF.
  IF l_changing_ko = abap_true.
    MESSAGE 'Function module Z_COLLECT_STATS has incorrect changing parameters. Check the installation instructions in SAP Note 1872170.' TYPE 'E'. "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.
  IF lt_tabparam IS NOT INITIAL.
    MESSAGE 'Function module Z_COLLECT_STATS has incorrect table parameters. Check the installation instructions in SAP Note 1872170.' TYPE 'E'. "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.
ENDFORM.                    " check_install

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  output_on_screen
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       Create output spool
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*

FORM output_on_screen USING outmode
                            "totals
                            l_cs_total l_rs_total l_hl l_hlch
                            l_disk l_init_data l_init_ws l_init_size
                            l_twocs
                            "NSE
                            l_paged l_paged_cache
                            "Additional components
                            l_indx l_lc l_s4_tr
                            "Simple Finance
                            l_sfincold l_coldsfinch l_sfintab l_sfincol
                            l_sfinnew l_fin_unl l_obs_fin
                            l_pca  " actually no longer regarded as part of Simple Finance
                            l_delcoep l_sl
                            "Simple Logistics
                            l_slogtab l_slogcol
                            l_log_chgvbfa l_log_oldvbfa l_log_newvbfa
                            l_slognew
                            l_log_unl l_log_les l_obs_log
                            "Material ledger actual costing
                            l_mlnew l_obs_ml
                            "Archiving,nse
                            l_elarch
                            l_pageable l_pageable_cache
                            "S/4 optimization
                            l_opt_data l_opt_ws l_optdisk l_opt_size
                            l_opt_twocs
                            "soh to S/4 optimizations
                            l_lraw2hl_gain l_lraw2hl_hl_growth
                            l_rs2cs_cs_growth l_rs2cs_rs_gain
                            l_opt_hlch l_opt_hl l_hl_rs2cs_growth
                            "persistent memory
                            l_init_pers l_init_dram
*                            l_opt_pers l_opt_dram
                            "details
                            l_cs_col l_cs_mlob l_cs_k   l_cs_pk
                            l_cs_hcard l_cs_mcard
                            l_cs_lcard l_cs_ucard
                            l_cs_rid l_cs_udiv l_cs_uk  l_cs_nuk
                            l_rs_col l_rs_mlob l_rs_pk  l_rs_sk
                            l_cshl   l_rshl
                            l_cs_jec l_cs_aging l_cs_ft
                            "in-place upgrade
                            l_updisk l_updata l_upchrec l_uptotal
                            l_shadisk l_sha l_shatotal
                            "technical details
                            l_wa_techd TYPE ty_techd
                            "business data
                            l_cl_lis
                            "errors
                            l_error_ratio.

  DATA: sizefield     TYPE fieldname,
        hlfield       TYPE fieldname,
        pkfield       TYPE fieldname,
        pagefield     TYPE fieldname,
        arobjcnt      TYPE i,
        arobjcnt_c(2) TYPE c.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS:
    <sizefs>  TYPE ty_hana_db_size-est_size,
    <hlfs>    TYPE ty_hana_db_size-est_hl_size,
    <cpu_per> TYPE ty_cpu_per.

  MESSAGE 'Creating spool output' TYPE 'S'.                 "#EC NOTEXT
  "TOP TABLE
  WRITE /.
  WRITE / c_line.
  mc_sp_t 'SIZING RESULTS IN GiB'.                          "#EC NOTEXT
  WRITE / c_line.
  mc_sp_t 'The anticipated maximum requirements for the HANA DATABASE SERVER are:'. "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sp_t space.
  IF l_wa_techd-basis_753 = abap_true.
    mc_sp_t 'for S/4HANA:'.                                 "#EC NOTEXT
  ELSE.
    IF l_wa_techd-db_vendor = 'HDB'.
      mc_sp_t 'for the analysed HANA system:'.              "#EC NOTEXT
    ELSE.
      mc_sp_t 'for a migration to HANA:'.                   "#EC NOTEXT
    ENDIF.
  ENDIF.
  mc_spn '- Memory requirement' l_init_size.                "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_spn '- Net data volume size on disk' l_disk.           "#EC NOTEXT
  IF wa_cpu_x-est_sapscnt >= 500000.
    mc_sp '- SAPS category' 'XXL'.                          "#EC NOTEXT
  ELSE.
    mc_sp '- SAPS category' wa_cpu_x-est_sapsts.            "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.
  IF l_opt_size IS NOT INITIAL AND ( l_opt_size <> l_init_size OR l_optdisk <> l_disk ).
    mc_sp_t space.
    mc_spn '- Memory requirement after optimization' l_opt_size. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_spn '- Net data volume size on disk after optimization' l_optdisk. "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.

  IF l_cl_lis IS NOT INITIAL.
    mc_sp_t space.
    mc_spn '- Memory requirement of client-dependent data' l_cl_lis. "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.

  " IF l_shatotal > 0 AND p_ful = abap_true.
  "   mc_sp_t space.
  "   mc_sp_t 'for an upgrade shadow instance:'.              "#EC NOTEXT
  "   mc_spn '- Memory requirement' l_shatotal.               "#EC NOTEXT
  "   mc_spn '- Data volume disk requirement' l_shadisk.      "#EC NOTEXT
  " ENDIF.
  IF l_uptotal > 0 AND p_ful = abap_true.
    mc_sp_t space.
    mc_sp_t 'for sMIG conversion to S/4HANA:'.              "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_spn '- Total additional memory requirement ' l_uptotal. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_spn '- Total additional data volume disk requirement' l_updisk.  "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.

  IF l_indx IS NOT INITIAL OR l_lc IS NOT INITIAL.  " OR l_s4_tr IS NOT INITIAL OR l_shatotal IS NOT INITIAL.
    mc_sp_t space.
    mc_sp_t 'Other possible additional memory requirement:'. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_spn '- for de-clustering of PCLx tables as per Note 1774918' l_indx. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_spn '- for the Live Cache' l_lc.                     "#EC NOTEXT
    " mc_spn '- during the transition to S/4HANA (See FAQ)' l_s4_tr."#EC NOTEXT
    " mc_spn '- for an upgrade shadow instance'  l_shatotal.  "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.
  WRITE / c_line.

  "GENERAL INFORMATION.
  WRITE / ' Check the FAQ document attached to SAP Note 1872170 for explanations on how'. "#EC NOTEXT
  WRITE: ' to interpret the sizing terms and calculations.', /. "#EC NOTEXT
  IF wa_cpu_x-est_sapscnt >= 300000.
    WRITE / ' The CPU Sizing is larger than 300.000 SAPS. Expert sizing is recommended.'. "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.

  IF wa_cpu_x-est_sapscnt IS INITIAL AND sy-dbsys(3) <> 'HDB'.
    WRITE: / ' No statistics were found. CPU sizing was not possible', /. "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.

  IF p_norm = abap_false.
    WRITE / ' This output has been recreated from a previous execution of the sizing report.'. "#EC NOTEXT
    WRITE: / ' Some detail information is missing.', /.     "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.

  IF l_wa_techd-db_vendor(3) = 'ADA' AND wa_techd-prec <> 'H'.
    WRITE / ' The sizing report has been executed on MaxDB with low or medium accuracy.'. "#EC NOTEXT
    WRITE / ' Since sampling is not possible with MaxDB, we recommend choosing a sample'. "#EC NOTEXT
    WRITE: / ' size of 1.000.000.', /.                      "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.

  mc_s 'Sizing report:' l_wa_techd-report_name.             "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_s 'Version of the report:' l_wa_techd-report_version.  "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_s 'Date of analysis:' l_wa_techd-crdate.               "#EC NOTEXT
  IF p_ocpu = abap_true.
    mc_s 'Date of CPU analysis:' sy-datum.                  "#EC NOTEXT
  ELSE.
    mc_s 'Date of CPU analysis:' l_wa_techd-crdate.         "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.
  IF l_wa_techd-db_vendor <> 'HDB' OR p_calib = abap_true.
    mc_s 'Selected sample size:' wa_techd-prec.             "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.
  IF l_wa_techd-db_vendor <> 'HDB' OR p_calib = abap_true.
    mc_s 'Cluster sampling mode:' wa_techd-clustprec.       "#EC NOTEXT
    IF wa_techd-taana_used = abap_true.
      mc_s 'TAANA results used:' 'Yes'.                     "#EC NOTEXT
      mc_s 'TAANA results used for clusters if not older than (days):' wa_techd-taana. "#EC NOTEXT
    ELSE.
      mc_s 'TAANA results used:' 'No'.                      "#EC NOTEXT
    ENDIF.
  ENDIF.
  mc_s 'Number of work processes used:' l_wa_techd-paral.   "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sn 'Duration of the analysis in seconds:' l_wa_techd-duration. "#EC NOTEXT

  IF l_wa_techd-db_vendor = 'HDB'.
    IF l_wa_techd-hdbload = abap_true.
      mc_s 'Unloaded columns were loaded:' 'Yes'.           "#EC NOTEXT
    ELSE.
      mc_s 'Unloaded columns were loaded:' 'No'.            "#EC NOTEXT
    ENDIF.
    IF l_wa_techd-hl = abap_true.
      mc_s 'The size of Hybrid LOB on disk was read:' 'Yes'. "#EC NOTEXT
    ELSE.
      mc_s 'The size of Hybrid LOB on disk was read:' 'No'. "#EC NOTEXT
    ENDIF.
    IF l_wa_techd-mac = abap_true.
      mc_s 'Tables were merged and compressed if necessary:' 'Yes'. "#EC NOTEXT
    ELSE.
      mc_s 'Tables were merged and compressed if necessary:' 'No'. "#EC NOTEXT
    ENDIF.
    IF l_wa_techd-hdb_empty_tables = abap_false AND l_wa_techd-report_version >= '78'. "param new with V78
      mc_s 'Empty tables are included in the sizing:' 'No'. "#EC NOTEXT
    ELSE.
      mc_s 'Empty tables are included in the sizing:' 'Yes'. "#EC NOTEXT
    ENDIF.
  ENDIF.

  IF l_wa_techd-calib = abap_true.
    mc_s 'Calibration:' outmode.                            "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.
  WRITE /.
  mc_s 'SID' l_wa_techd-sid.                                "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_s 'NW release:' l_wa_techd-sapversion.                 "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_s 'Kernel version' l_wa_techd-kernversion.             "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_s 'Operating system on AS' l_wa_techd-osversion(19).   "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_s 'Type of analysed database:' l_wa_techd-db_vendor.   "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_s 'Database version:' l_wa_techd-db_release.           "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_s 'Unicode system:' l_wa_techd-unicode.                "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sn 'Data used size on disk of the analysed database in GiB:' wa_techd-anydbsize_n. "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_s 'Date of last disk size analysis (See FAQ):' wa_techd-anydbsizedate. "#EC NOTEXT

  WRITE /.
  mc_sn 'Number of tables successfully analysed:' l_wa_techd-success_cnt. "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sn 'Number of tables partially analysed:' l_wa_techd-partial_cnt. "#EC NOTEXT
  "Always write error count even if initial.
  WRITE: / '', AT 2 'Number of tables with error:', AT 63(17) l_wa_techd-error_cnt RIGHT-JUSTIFIED. "#EC NOTEXT

  IF l_wa_techd-lcerror = abap_true.
    WRITE /.
    mc_s 'Live Cache sizing was not possible:' 'See FAQ'.   "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.

  IF l_wa_techd-mss1691513 = abap_true.
    WRITE / ' IMPORTANT: On MSSQL and NW 700, SAP Note 1691513 MUST be implemented before'. "#EC NOTEXT
    WRITE / ' running the sizing report.'.                  "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.

  "ERRORS TABLE
  IF gt_error IS NOT INITIAL.
    SORT gt_error BY db_table.
    IF l_error_ratio > 0.
      mc_sn 'Error estimation in % due to tables with errors:' l_error_ratio. "#EC NOTEXT
    ENDIF.
    IF l_error_ratio > c_max_err OR l_init_data = 0.
      WRITE /.
      WRITE: / '', AT 2 'WARNING! The size of tables in error is', "#EC NOTEXT
             'too large. The sizing result is NOT reliable. Check the', "#EC NOTEXT
             ' error log, correct the errors and re-execute the report.' RIGHT-JUSTIFIED. "#EC NOTEXT
    ENDIF.
    WRITE /.

    " Write errors
    WRITE / c_big_line.
    WRITE: / '|', (30) 'TABLES NAMES', (67) 'ERROR MESSAGE/CODE (See FAQ)' LEFT-JUSTIFIED, AT 101 '|'. "#EC NOTEXT
    WRITE / c_big_line.
    LOOP AT gt_error INTO ls_error.
      WRITE: / '|', (30) ls_error-table_name.
      IF ls_error-error_message IS NOT INITIAL.
        WRITE: (67) ls_error-error_message LEFT-JUSTIFIED, AT 101 '|'.
      ELSE.
        WRITE: (67) ls_error-return_code   LEFT-JUSTIFIED, AT 101 '|'.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.
    WRITE / c_big_line.
  ENDIF.

  "Partial collection
  IF gt_partial IS NOT INITIAL.
    SORT gt_partial BY db_table.
    WRITE /.
    WRITE / c_line.
    WRITE: / '|', AT 3 'TABLES PARTIALLY READ', AT 53 'NUMBER OF RECORDS SAMPLED' CENTERED, AT 80 '|'. "#EC NOTEXT
    WRITE / c_line.
    LOOP AT gt_partial INTO ls_partial.
      WRITE: / '|', AT 3  ls_partial-table_name, AT 53 ls_partial-records_sampled LEFT-JUSTIFIED, AT 80 '|'.
    ENDLOOP.
    WRITE / c_line.
  ENDIF.

  "INIT DETAILS TABLE
  WRITE /.
  WRITE / c_line.
  mc_t2 'MEMORY SIZING CALCULATION DETAILS' 'HANA SIZE IN GiB'. "#EC NOTEXT
  WRITE / c_line.
  mc_sp '  Column loadable data' l_cs_total.                   "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sp ' (Of which is added due to conversion from Row Store)' l_rs2cs_cs_growth.  "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sp '+ Row Store data' l_rs_total.                      "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sp ' (of which is removed due to conversion to Column Store)' l_rs2cs_rs_gain.    "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sp ' (Including concatenated attributes not from DDIC)' l_cs_jec. "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sp '+ Changes in FI tables and columns' l_sfinnew.     "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sp '+ Changes in MM/SD tables and columns' l_slognew.  "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sp '+ Changes in ML tables and columns' l_mlnew.       "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sep_line.

  mc_sp '= Memory requirement for the initial loadable data' l_init_data. "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sp '+ Hybrid LOB cache (10% of size on disk)' l_hlch.  "#EC NOTEXT
  outln = c_nse_ratio.
  CONDENSE outln.
  CONCATENATE '+ NSE cache for page loadable data (1/' outln ' of size on disk)' INTO outln. "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sp outln l_paged_cache.

  mc_sp '+ Work space (100% Column + 50% Row Store)' l_init_ws. "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sp '+ Fixed size for code, stack and other services' codestack. "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sep_line.

  mc_sp '= Anticipated initial memory requirement' l_init_size. "#EC NOTEXT
  WRITE / c_line.

  "DISK SIZING DETAILS.
  WRITE /.
  WRITE / c_line.
  mc_t2 'DISK SIZING CALCULATION DETAILS' 'HANA SIZE IN GiB'. "#EC NOTEXT
  WRITE / c_line.
  mc_sp '  Column loadable data' l_cs_total.                "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sp '+ Row Store data' l_rs_total.                      "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sp '+ Changes in FI tables' l_sfinnew.                 "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sp '+ Changes in MM/SD tables' l_slognew.              "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sp '+ Changes in ML tables' l_mlnew.                   "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sp '+ Hybrid LOBs' l_hl.                               "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sp '+ Page loadable data (NSE)' l_paged.               "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sp '+ Space required for merges' l_twocs.              "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sp '+ Metadata and statistics' diskadmin.              "#EC NOTEXT
  mc_sep_line.
  mc_sp '= Initial net data size on disk' l_disk.           "#EC NOTEXT
  WRITE / c_line.
  WRITE /.

  "OPTIMIZATION DETAILS TABLE
  IF l_opt_size <> l_init_size OR l_optdisk <> l_disk.
    WRITE / c_line.
    mc_t2 'MEMORY SIZING AFTER OPTIMIZATION' 'HANA SIZE IN GiB'. "#EC NOTEXT
    WRITE / c_line.
    mc_sp '  Memory requirement for the initial loadable data' l_init_data. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp '- Obsolete financial data (Aggregates, indexes...)' l_obs_fin. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp '- Obsolete logistics data (Aggregates, indexes...)' l_obs_log. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp '- Obsolete material ledger actual costing data' l_obs_ml. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp '- Data convertible to paged loadable (NSE)' l_pageable. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp '- Obsolete non-unique secondary indexes' l_cs_jec. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp '- Columns converted to hybrid LOB' l_lraw2hl_gain. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sep_line.
    mc_sp '= Memory requirement for data after optimization' l_opt_data. "#EC NOTEXT
    outln = c_nse_ratio.
    CONDENSE outln.
    CONCATENATE '+ NSE cache for page loadable data (1/' outln ' of size on disk)' INTO outln. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp outln l_paged_cache.
    mc_sp '+ NSE cache for data convertible to paged loadable' l_pageable_cache. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp '+ Cached Hybrid LOB (10% of size on disk)' l_opt_hlch. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp '+ Work space (100% Column + 50% Row Store)' l_opt_ws. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp '+ Fixed size for code, stack and other services' codestack. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sep_line.
    mc_sp '= Anticipated memory requirement after optimization' l_opt_size. "#EC NOTEXT
    WRITE / c_line.
    WRITE /.
    "END OF OPTIMIZATION DETAILS TABLE

    "OPT DISK SIZING DETAILS.
    WRITE / c_line.
    mc_t2 'DISK SIZING AFTER OPTIMIZATION' 'HANA SIZE IN GiB'. "#EC NOTEXT
    WRITE / c_line.
    mc_sp '  Column loadable data after optimization' l_opt_data. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp '+ Page loadable data (NSE)' l_paged.             "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp '+ Page loadable data convertible to (NSE)' l_pageable. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp '+ Hybrid LOBs' l_opt_hl.                         "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp '+ Space required for merges' l_opt_twocs.        "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp '+ Metadata and statistics' diskadmin.            "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sep_line.
    mc_sp '= Net data size on disk after optimization' l_optdisk. "#EC NOTEXT
    WRITE / c_line.
    WRITE /.
    WRITE /.

    "START OF S/4 DETAILS TABLE
    WRITE / c_line.
    mc_t2 'OPTIMIZATION CALCULATION DETAILS' 'HANA SIZE IN GiB'. "#EC NOTEXT
    WRITE / c_line.
    " To Simple Finance
    mc_sp1 'Changes in FI tables and columns' l_sfinnew.    "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp1 '  New financial tables:'          l_sfintab.    "#EC NOTEXT
    LOOP AT gt_sfin2 ASSIGNING <sfin> WHERE table_name(6) = 'ACDOCA'.
      CONCATENATE <sfin>-table_name <sfin>-group INTO outln SEPARATED BY space.
      mc_spi outln <sfin>-ssize.
    ENDLOOP.
    LOOP AT gt_sfin2 ASSIGNING <sfin> WHERE group = 'FI-AA'.
      mc_spi <sfin>-table_name <sfin>-ssize.
    ENDLOOP.
    mc_sp1 '  New columns in existing tables:' l_sfincol.   "#EC NOTEXT
    LOOP AT gt_sfin2 ASSIGNING <sfin> WHERE group = 'NEWCOL' AND size > 0.
      mc_spi <sfin>-table_name <sfin>-ssize.
    ENDLOOP.
    IF l_sfinnew IS NOT INITIAL.
      mc_sp_t space.
    ENDIF.

    "To Simple Logistics
    mc_sp1 'Changes in logistics tables and columns' l_slognew. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp1 ' - New tables:' l_slogtab.                      "#EC NOTEXT
    LOOP AT gt_slog ASSIGNING <slog> WHERE group = 'TAB' AND ssize > 0.
      mc_spi <slog>-table_name <slog>-ssize.
    ENDLOOP.
    mc_sp1 ' - New columns in existing tables:' l_slogcol.  "#EC NOTEXT
    LOOP AT gt_slog ASSIGNING <slog> WHERE group = 'NEWCOL' AND ssize > 0.
      mc_spi <slog>-table_name <slog>-ssize.
    ENDLOOP.
    mc_sp1 ' - Changes in VBFA:' l_log_chgvbfa.             "#EC NOTEXT
    IF l_log_chgvbfa IS NOT INITIAL.
      mc_spi 'Old VBFA table' l_log_oldvbfa.                "#EC NOTEXT
      mc_spi 'New VBFA table' l_log_newvbfa.                "#EC NOTEXT
    ENDIF.
    IF l_slognew IS NOT INITIAL.
      mc_sp_t space.
    ENDIF.

    "To new actual costing
    mc_sp1 'Changes in actual costing tables' l_mlnew.      "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp1 ' - New tables:' l_mlnew.                        "#EC NOTEXT
    LOOP AT gt_ml ASSIGNING <ml> WHERE group = 'AC' AND ssize > 0.
      mc_spi <ml>-table_name <ml>-ssize.
    ENDLOOP.
    IF l_mlnew IS NOT INITIAL.
      mc_sp_t space.
    ENDIF.

    "Saving potential with Simple Finance
    mc_sp1 'Obsolete financial data' l_obs_fin.             "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp1 ' - Obsolete tables to unload:' l_fin_unl.       "#EC NOTEXT
    LOOP AT gt_sfin2 ASSIGNING <sfin>
      WHERE ( group = 'UNLOAD' OR group = 'NEWGL' OR group = 'AA' OR group = 'FAAT' ) AND size > 0.
      mc_spi <sfin>-table_name <sfin>-size.
    ENDLOOP.
    mc_sp1 ' - Tables moved to historical partitions:' l_sfincold. "#EC NOTEXT
    LOOP AT gt_sfin2 ASSIGNING <sfin> WHERE group = 'INDEX' AND size > 0.
      mc_spi <sfin>-table_name <sfin>-size.
    ENDLOOP.
    mc_sp1 ' - Deletion of obsolete CO documents:' l_delcoep. "#EC NOTEXT
    LOOP AT gt_sfin2 ASSIGNING <sfin> WHERE ( group = 'OBSCO' OR table_name = 'COEP' ) AND size > 0.
      mc_spi <sfin>-table_name <sfin>-osize.
    ENDLOOP.
    mc_sp1 ' - Phase-out of Special Ledgers (FI-SL):' l_sl. "#EC NOTEXT
    LOOP AT gt_sfin2 ASSIGNING <sfin> WHERE group = 'FI-SL' AND size > 0.
      mc_spi <sfin>-table_name <sfin>-size.
    ENDLOOP.
    IF l_obs_fin IS NOT INITIAL.
      mc_sp_t space.
    ENDIF.

    mc_sp1 'Obsolete Classic Profit Center Accounting data' l_pca. "#EC NOTEXT
    LOOP AT gt_ec_pca ASSIGNING <ec_pca> WHERE group = 'EC-PCA' AND size > 0.
      mc_spi <ec_pca>-table_name <ec_pca>-size.
    ENDLOOP.

    "Saving potential with Simple Logistics
    mc_sp1 'Obsolete logistics data' l_obs_log.             "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp1 ' - Obsolete tables:' l_log_unl.                 "#EC NOTEXT
    LOOP AT gt_slog ASSIGNING <slog> WHERE group = 'UNLOAD' AND size > 0.
      mc_spi <slog>-table_name <slog>-size.
    ENDLOOP.
    mc_sp1 ' - Obsolete columns in tables:' l_log_les.      "#EC NOTEXT
    LOOP AT gt_slog ASSIGNING <slog> WHERE group = 'LESS' AND ssize > 0.
      mc_spi <slog>-table_name <slog>-ssize.
    ENDLOOP.
    IF l_obs_log IS NOT INITIAL.
      mc_sp_t space.
    ENDIF.

    "Saving potential with actual costing
    mc_sp1 'Obsolete actual costing data' l_obs_ml.         "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp1 ' - Obsolete tables:' l_obs_ml.                  "#EC NOTEXT
    LOOP AT gt_ml ASSIGNING <ml> WHERE group = 'OBS' AND ssize > 0.
      mc_spi <ml>-table_name <ml>-ssize.
    ENDLOOP.
    IF l_obs_ml IS NOT INITIAL.
      mc_sp_t space.
    ENDIF.

    "NSE
    IF l_pageable IS NOT INITIAL.
      mc_sp1 'Column loadable tables convertible to page loadable (NSE):' l_pageable. "#EC NOTEXT
      SORT gt_tables BY opt_pageable_size DESCENDING.
      LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item>.
        ADD 1 TO count.
        IF count > p_topobj OR <item>-opt_pageable_size = 0.
          EXIT.
        ENDIF.
        mc_spi <item>-table_name <item>-opt_pageable_size.
      ENDLOOP.
      CLEAR count.
      mc_sp_t space.
    ENDIF.

    "Non-unique keys in DDIC
    IF l_cs_nuk IS NOT INITIAL.
      mc_sp1 'Obsolete non-unique secondary indexes' l_cs_nuk. "#EC NOTEXT
      mc_sp1 'Obsolete concatenated secondary indexes' l_cs_jec. "#EC NOTEXT
      mc_sp_t 'Check SAP Note 1986747 to identify the obsolete indexes.'. "#EC NOTEXT
    ENDIF.
    "LRAW to HL conversion
    IF l_lraw2hl_gain > 0.
      mc_sp1 'Memory usage reduction with LRAW conversion to Hybrid LOB' l_lraw2hl_gain. "#EC NOTEXT
      mc_sp_t '- The list of tables with LRAW colums is displayed in a separate table.'.  "#EC NOTEXT
    ENDIF.
    WRITE / c_line.
    WRITE /.

    IF l_obs_fin > 0.
      WRITE / ' Refer to SAP Note 2818267 for DVM recommendations during migration to S/4HANA.'. "#EC NOTEXT
    ENDIF.
  ENDIF.

  "CPU sizing details
  IF wa_cpu_x IS NOT INITIAL.
    WRITE / c_line.
    mc_sp_t 'CPU SIZING DETAILS'.                           "#EC NOTEXT
    WRITE / c_line.
    mc_sp 'Available aggregated statistics basis:' 'Intervals'. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_per 'H' 'Hourly'.                                    "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_per 'D' 'Daily'.                                     "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_per 'W' 'Weekly'.                                    "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_per 'M' 'Monthly'.                                   "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp_t space.
    mc_spn 'Peak (Select equivalent/h)' wa_cpu_x-max_hloadcnt. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp 'Peak period basis' wa_cpu_x-datecnt.             "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_spn 'Peak Factor' wa_cpu_x-max_factcnt.              "#EC NOTEXT
    "  mc_sp 'Peak Factor date' wa_cpu_x-max_factcnt_date.  "#EC NOTEXT
    IF wa_cpu_x-est_sapscnt >= 500000.
      mc_sp 'Estimated SAPS' 'N/A'.                         "#EC NOTEXT
    ELSE.
      mc_spn 'Estimated SAPS' wa_cpu_x-est_sapscnt.         "#EC NOTEXT
    ENDIF.
    mc_sp 'Estimated SAPS category' wa_cpu_x-est_sapsts.    "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_spn 'Peak period background tasks percentage' wa_cpu_x-bkgratio. "#EC NOTEXT
    WRITE / c_line.
    IF wa_cpu_x-bkgratio >= 50.
      WRITE / ' The share of background jobs in the load is above 50%. The CPU Sizing'. "#EC NOTEXT
      WRITE: / ' estimation is possibly too high.', /.      "#EC NOTEXT
    ENDIF.
    WRITE / ' Check the FAQ document attached to SAP Note 1872170 for explanations on how'. "#EC NOTEXT
    WRITE: ' to interpret the CPU sizing calculations.', /. "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.

  "SIZING FOR NVRAM
  IF l_init_pers IS NOT INITIAL AND l_wa_techd-is_pers_mem = abap_true.
    WRITE / c_line.
    mc_t2 'PERSISTENT MEMORY SIZING' 'HANA SIZE IN GiB'.    "#EC NOTEXT
    WRITE / c_line.
    mc_sp '  Column Store data' l_cs_total.                 "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp '+ Changes in FI tables and columns' l_sfinnew.   "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp '+ Changes in MM/SD tables and columns' l_slognew. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp '+ Changes in ML tables and columns' l_mlnew.     "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sep_line.
    mc_sp '= Persistent Memory (NVRAM) initial requirement' l_init_pers. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp_t space.
    mc_sp '  Row store data' l_rs_total.                    "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp '+ Cached Hybrid LOB (10%)' l_hlch.               "#EC NOTEXT
    outln = c_nse_ratio.
    CONDENSE outln.
    CONCATENATE '+ NSE cache for page loadable data (1/' outln ' of size on disk)' INTO outln. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp outln l_paged_cache.
    mc_sp '+ Work space' l_init_ws.                         "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sp '+ Fixed size for code, stack and other services' codestack. "#EC NOTEXT
    mc_sep_line.
    mc_sp '= Volatile memory (DRAM) initial requirement' l_init_dram. "#EC NOTEXT
    WRITE / c_line.
    WRITE /.
  ENDIF.

  IF outmode = 'ANY'.
    sizefield = 'EST_SIZE'.
    hlfield   = 'EST_HL_SIZE'.
    pkfield   = 'EST_PK_SIZE'.
    pagefield = 'EST_PAGED_SIZE'.
  ELSE.
    sizefield = 'REAL_SIZE'.
    hlfield   = 'REAL_HL_SIZE'.
    pkfield   = 'REAL_PK_SIZE'.
    pagefield = 'REAL_PAGED_SIZE'.
  ENDIF.

  " LARGEST CS TABLES
  CLEAR: gt_top, gs_top,  count.
  SORT gt_tables BY (sizefield) DESCENDING record_count DESCENDING.
  LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WHERE store = 'CS' AND load_unit <> 'PAGE'.
    ADD 1 TO count.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT sizefield OF STRUCTURE <item> TO <sizefs>.
    IF count > p_topobj OR ( gt_nso IS INITIAL AND <sizefs> = 0 ).
      EXIT.
    ENDIF.
    gs_top-col1  = <item>-table_name.
    gs_top-col2p = <sizefs>.
    gs_top-col3d = <item>-record_count.
    APPEND gs_top TO gt_top.
  ENDLOOP.
  mc_topheader '  LARGEST COLUMN' ' LOADABLE TABLES'
               ' ESTIMATED MEMORY' '    SIZE IN GiB'
               'ESTIMATED RECORD' '      COUNT'.            "#EC NOTEXT
  PERFORM list_top_objects TABLES gt_top USING 'pd'.

  "Page loadable data
  CLEAR: gt_top, gs_top, count.
  SORT gt_tables BY (pagefield) DESCENDING record_count DESCENDING.
  LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WHERE load_unit = 'PAGE'.
    ADD 1 TO count.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT pagefield OF STRUCTURE <item> TO <sizefs>.
    IF count > p_topobj OR ( gt_nso IS INITIAL AND <sizefs> = 0 ).
      EXIT.
    ENDIF.
    gs_top-col1  = <item>-table_name.
    gs_top-col2p = <sizefs>.
    gs_top-col3d = <item>-record_count.
    APPEND gs_top TO gt_top.
  ENDLOOP.
  IF count IS NOT INITIAL.
    mc_topheader '  LARGEST PAGE' 'LOADABLE TABLES'
                 'ESTIMATED DISK' '  SIZE IN GiB'
                 'ESTIMATED RECORD' '      COUNT'.          "#EC NOTEXT
    PERFORM list_top_objects TABLES gt_top USING 'pd'.
  ENDIF.

  " LARGEST CS PK
  IF l_cs_pk > 0.
    CLEAR: gt_top, gs_top, count.
    SORT gt_tables BY (pkfield) DESCENDING record_count DESCENDING.
    LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WHERE store = 'CS'.
      ADD 1 TO count.
      ASSIGN COMPONENT pkfield OF STRUCTURE <item> TO <sizefs>.
      IF count > p_topobj OR <sizefs> = 0.
        EXIT.
      ENDIF.
      gs_top-col1  = <item>-table_name.
      gs_top-col2p = <sizefs>.
      ASSIGN COMPONENT sizefield OF STRUCTURE <item> TO <sizefs>.
      gs_top-col3p = <sizefs>.
      APPEND gs_top TO gt_top.
    ENDLOOP.
    mc_topheader 'LARGEST COLUMN STORE' '  PRIMARY KEYS'
                 ' PRIMARY KEY ' 'MEMORY SIZE IN GiB'
                 '    ENTIRE TABLE' '      SIZE IN GiB'. "#EC NOTEXT
    PERFORM list_top_objects TABLES gt_top USING 'pp'.
  ENDIF.

  IF l_cs_jec > 0. "Concatenated attributes
    CLEAR: gt_top, gs_top, count.
    SORT gt_tables BY real_jec_size DESCENDING record_count DESCENDING.
    LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WHERE store = 'CS'.
      ADD 1 TO count.
      IF count > p_topobj OR <item>-real_jec_size = 0.
        EXIT.
      ENDIF.
      gs_top-col1  = <item>-table_name.
      gs_top-col2p = <item>-real_jec_size.
      ASSIGN COMPONENT sizefield OF STRUCTURE <item> TO <sizefs>.
      gs_top-col3p = <sizefs>.
      APPEND gs_top TO gt_top.
    ENDLOOP.
    mc_topheader ' LARGEST NON-DDIC' 'CONCAT. ATTRIBUTES'
                 'CONCAT. ATTRIBUTES' '    SIZE IN GiB'
                 '    OTHER COLUMNS' '     SIZE IN GiB'.    "#EC NOTEXT
    PERFORM list_top_objects TABLES gt_top USING 'pp'.
    IF gt_top IS NOT INITIAL. "read older report case
      WRITE ' Check with SAP Note 1986747 if the above concatenated attributes are necessary.'. "#EC NOTEXT
    ENDIF.
  ENDIF.

  IF l_cs_nuk > 0. "non-unique indexes
    CLEAR: gt_top, gs_top, count.
    SORT gt_tables BY real_nuk_size DESCENDING record_count DESCENDING.
    LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WHERE store = 'CS'.
      ADD 1 TO count.
      IF count > p_topobj OR <item>-real_nuk_size = 0.
        EXIT.
      ENDIF.
      gs_top-col1  = <item>-table_name.
      gs_top-col2p = <item>-real_nuk_size.
      ASSIGN COMPONENT sizefield OF STRUCTURE <item> TO <sizefs>.
      gs_top-col3p = <sizefs>.
      APPEND gs_top TO gt_top.
    ENDLOOP.
    mc_topheader ' LARGEST NON'    'UNIQUE INDEXES'
                 'CONCAT. ATTRIBUTES' '    SIZE IN GiB'
                 '    ENTIRE TABLE' '     SIZE IN GiB'.     "#EC NOTEXT
    PERFORM list_top_objects TABLES gt_top USING 'pp'.
  ENDIF.

  IF l_cs_ft > 0. "ESH attributes
    CLEAR: gt_top, gs_top, count.
    SORT gt_tables BY real_esh_size DESCENDING record_count DESCENDING.
    LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WHERE store = 'CS'.
      ADD 1 TO count.
      IF count > p_topobj OR <item>-real_esh_size = 0.
        EXIT.
      ENDIF.
      gs_top-col1  = <item>-table_name.
      gs_top-col2p = <item>-real_esh_size.
      ASSIGN COMPONENT sizefield OF STRUCTURE <item> TO <sizefs>.
      gs_top-col3p = <sizefs>.
      APPEND gs_top TO gt_top.
    ENDLOOP.
    mc_topheader ' LARGEST ENTERPRISE' 'SEARCH ATTRIBUTES'
                 'MEMORY SIZE IN GiB' ''
                 '    ENTIRE TABLE' '     SIZE IN GiB'.     "#EC NOTEXT
    PERFORM list_top_objects TABLES gt_top USING 'pp'.
  ENDIF.

  " LARGEST RS TABLES
  CLEAR: gt_top, gs_top,  count.
  SORT gt_tables BY (sizefield) DESCENDING record_count DESCENDING.
  LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WHERE store = 'RS'.
    ADD 1 TO count.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT sizefield OF STRUCTURE <item> TO <sizefs>.
    IF count > p_topobj OR ( gt_nso IS INITIAL AND <sizefs> = 0 ).
      EXIT.
    ENDIF.
    gs_top-col1  = <item>-table_name.
    gs_top-col2p = <sizefs>.
    gs_top-col3d = <item>-record_count.
    APPEND gs_top TO gt_top.
  ENDLOOP.
  mc_topheader ' LARGEST ROW' 'STORE TABLES'
               'ESTIMATED MEMORY' '     SIZE IN GiB'
               'ESTIMATED RECORD' '      COUNT'. "#EC NOTEXT
  PERFORM list_top_objects TABLES gt_top USING 'pd'.

  IF l_lraw2hl_gain > 0.
    "Conversion from LRAW to HL
    CLEAR: gt_top, gs_top, count.
    SORT gt_soh2s4 BY soh_size DESCENDING.
    LOOP AT gt_soh2s4 ASSIGNING <soh2s4> WHERE reason = 'LRAW2HL'.
      ADD 1 TO count.
      IF count > p_topobj OR <soh2s4>-soh_size > 0.
        EXIT.
      ENDIF.
      gs_top-col1  = <soh2s4>-table_name.
      gs_top-col2p = <soh2s4>-soh_size.
      gs_top-col3p = <soh2s4>-opt_size.
      APPEND gs_top TO gt_top.
    ENDLOOP.
    mc_topheader 'TABLES WITH' ' LRAW COLUMNS'
                 ' CURRENT MEMORY' '   SIZE IN GiB'
                 'ESTIMATED MEMORY' '   SIZE IN GiB'. "#EC NOTEXT
    PERFORM list_top_objects TABLES gt_top USING 'pp'.
    WRITE ' After an upgrade to SAP_BASIS >= 7.53 on HANA the previous VARBINARY columns'. "#EC NOTEXT
    WRITE: / ' remain in place until an ABAP table conversion happens. See SAP Note 2220627.', /. "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.

  IF l_rs2cs_rs_gain > 0.
    "Conversion from RS to CS
    CLEAR: gt_top, gs_top, count.
    SORT gt_soh2s4 BY soh_size DESCENDING.
    LOOP AT gt_soh2s4 ASSIGNING <soh2s4> WHERE reason = 'RS2CS'.
      ADD 1 TO count.
      IF count > p_topobj OR <soh2s4>-soh_size > 0.
        EXIT.
      ENDIF.
      gs_top-col1  = <soh2s4>-table_name.
      gs_top-col2p = <soh2s4>-soh_size.
      gs_top-col3p = <soh2s4>-opt_size.
      APPEND gs_top TO gt_top.
    ENDLOOP.
    mc_topheader '  ROW STORE TABLES' 'MOVED TO COL. STORE'
                 ' CURENT ROW STORE' ' MEMORY SIZE IN GiB'
                 '   EST. COL. SIZE' '     SIZE IN GiB'. "#EC NOTEXT
    PERFORM list_top_objects TABLES gt_top USING 'pp'.
    WRITE / ' During the transition to S/4HANA some tables are moved to the Column Store.'. "#EC NOTEXT
    WRITE: / ' The table above shows their estimated sizes in the Column Store.', /. "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.

  " IF l_shatotal > 0. "UPGRADE
  "   WRITE / c_line.
  "   mc_t2 'ESTIMATED REQUIREMENT FOR UPGRADE SHADOW INSTANCES' 'HANA SIZE IN GiB'. "#EC NOTEXT
  "   WRITE / c_line.
  "   mc_sp '  Estimated size of tables cloned to shadow instances' l_sha. "#EC NOTEXT
  "   mc_sp '+ Estimated corresponding work space requirement' l_sha. "#EC NOTEXT
  "   mc_sep_line.
  "   mc_sp '= Total memory requirement for shadow instances' l_shatotal. "#EC NOTEXT
  "   mc_sp '= Total disk requirement for shadow instances' l_shadisk. "#EC NOTEXT
  "   IF l_uptotal <> l_shatotal.
  "     mc_sp_t space.
  "     mc_sp '+ Estimated data size of cloned tables for sMIG conversion' l_updata. "#EC NOTEXT
  "     mc_sp '+ Estimated size of change recording and replay tables' l_upchrec. "#EC NOTEXT
  "     mc_sp '+ Estimated work space requirement for cloned tables' l_updata. "#EC NOTEXT
  "     mc_sep_line.
  "     mc_sp '= Total additional memory requirement for sMIG conversion' l_uptotal. "#EC NOTEXT
  "   ENDIF.
  "   WRITE / c_line.
  "   WRITE /.
  " ENDIF.

  IF l_cshl > 0 OR l_rshl > 0." largest LOB objects.
    CLEAR: gt_top, gs_top, count.

    LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item>.
      ADD 1 TO count.
      ASSIGN COMPONENT hlfield OF STRUCTURE <item> TO <hlfs>.
      IF count > p_topobj OR <hlfs> = 0.
        EXIT.
      ENDIF.
      gs_top-col1  = <item>-table_name.
      gs_top-col2p = <hlfs>.
      gs_top-col3d = <item>-record_count.
      APPEND gs_top TO gt_top.
