*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  SFIN_SIZING
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*

FORM sfin_sizing.
  DATA: ls_sfin2     TYPE ty_ssol,
        lv_newgl     TYPE dec20,
        lv_aa        TYPE dec20,
        lv_faat      TYPE dec20,
        ls_bseg      TYPE ty_ssol,
        ls_coep      TYPE ty_ssol,
        l_len        TYPE i,
        actual_ratio TYPE p LENGTH 9 DECIMALS 3,
        avg_acdoca   TYPE p LENGTH 9 DECIMALS 2.
  CONSTANTS newgl_t881 TYPE tabname VALUE 't881'.           "#EC NOTEXT

  LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WHERE store = 'CS'.
    CASE <item>-table_name.
        "sum tables and others..
      WHEN 'GLT0' OR 'GLT0_BCK' OR 'GLT0_DIF'
        OR 'FAGLFLEXT' OR 'FAGLFLEXT_BCK'
        OR 'KNC1' OR 'KNC3' OR 'LFC1' OR 'LFC3'
        OR 'BSIM' OR 'T012K'
        OR 'FMGLFLEXT' OR 'PSGLFLEXT' OR 'JVGLFLEXT'
        OR 'KNC1_BCK' OR 'KNC3_BCK' OR 'LFC1_BCK' OR 'LFC3_BCK'.
        ls_sfin2-group = 'UNLOAD'.
      WHEN 'BSID' OR 'BSIK' OR 'BSAD' OR 'BSAK' OR 'BSIS' OR 'BSAS'
        OR 'FAGLBSIS' OR 'FAGLBSAS'
        OR 'BSAS_BCK' OR 'BSIS_BCK' OR 'BSAK_BCK' OR 'BSIK_BCK' OR 'BSAD_BCK' OR 'BSID_BCK'. "indexes tables
        ls_sfin2-group = 'INDEX'.
      WHEN  'BSEG'.
        ls_sfin2-group = 'NEWCOL'.
      WHEN 'COEP'.
        READ TABLE <item>-cs_cols ASSIGNING <cs_size> WITH KEY column_name = 'WRTTP'.
        IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
          ls_sfin2-spec_count = <cs_size>-spec_count.
        ENDIF.
        ls_sfin2-group = 'NEWCOL'.
      WHEN 'COSP' OR 'COSS' OR 'COSS_BAK' OR 'COSP_BAK'.
        ls_sfin2-group = 'OBSCO'.
      WHEN 'ANEA' OR 'ANLC' OR 'ANEP'. "Asset Acc.
        ls_sfin2-group = 'AA'.
      WHEN 'ANEK' OR 'ANLP' .
        ls_sfin2-group = 'FAAT'.
    ENDCASE.
    IF ls_sfin2-group IS NOT INITIAL.
      MOVE-CORRESPONDING <item> TO ls_sfin2.
      IF sy-dbsys(3) = 'HDB'.
        ls_sfin2-size = <item>-real_size.
      ELSE.
        ls_sfin2-size = <item>-est_size.
      ENDIF.
      APPEND ls_sfin2 TO gt_sfin2.
      CLEAR ls_sfin2.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.

  SELECT DISTINCT tab FROM (newgl_t881) INTO ls_sfin2-table_name WHERE appl = 'FI' AND subappl IN ('GLF', 'PSM', 'PSX', 'JVA').
    IF ls_sfin2-table_name IS NOT INITIAL.
      l_len = strlen( ls_sfin2-table_name ) - 1.
      ls_sfin2-table_name+l_len = 'A'.
      READ TABLE gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WITH KEY table_name = ls_sfin2-table_name BINARY SEARCH.
      IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
        MOVE-CORRESPONDING <item> TO ls_sfin2.
        IF sy-dbsys(3) = 'HDB'.
          ls_sfin2-size = <item>-real_size.
        ELSE.
          ls_sfin2-size = <item>-est_size.
        ENDIF.
        ls_sfin2-group = 'NEWGL'.
        APPEND ls_sfin2 TO gt_sfin2.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.
    CLEAR ls_sfin2.
  ENDSELECT.

  SELECT DISTINCT tab FROM (newgl_t881) INTO ls_sfin2-table_name WHERE appl = 'FI' AND subappl = 'SL'.
    IF ls_sfin2-table_name IS NOT INITIAL.
      l_len = strlen( ls_sfin2-table_name ) - 1.
      ls_sfin2-table_name+l_len = 'A'.
      READ TABLE gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WITH KEY table_name = ls_sfin2-table_name BINARY SEARCH.
      IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
        "check that table is not already in gt_sfin2
        READ TABLE gt_sfin2 WITH KEY table_name = <item>-table_name TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS.
        IF sy-subrc IS NOT INITIAL.
          MOVE-CORRESPONDING <item> TO ls_sfin2.
          IF sy-dbsys(3) = 'HDB'.
            ls_sfin2-size = <item>-real_size.
          ELSE.
            ls_sfin2-size = <item>-est_size.
          ENDIF.
          ls_sfin2-group = 'FI-SL'.
          APPEND ls_sfin2 TO gt_sfin2.
        ENDIF.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.
    CLEAR ls_sfin2.
  ENDSELECT.


  LOOP AT gt_sfin2 ASSIGNING <sfin>.
    CASE <sfin>-group.
      WHEN 'INDEX'.
        est_sfincold = est_sfincold + <sfin>-size.
        LOOP AT <sfin>-cs_cols ASSIGNING <cs_size>.
          IF sy-dbsys(3) <> 'HDB'.
            est_sfin_inv = est_sfin_inv + <cs_size>-est_ms_index + <cs_size>-est_ms_misc.
          ELSE.
            est_sfin_inv = est_sfin_inv + <cs_size>-ms_index     + <cs_size>-ms_misc.
          ENDIF.
        ENDLOOP.
      WHEN 'UNLOAD'.
        est_fin_unl = est_fin_unl + <sfin>-size.
      WHEN 'NEWGL'.
        est_fin_unl = est_fin_unl + <sfin>-size.
        lv_newgl  = lv_newgl + <sfin>-record_count.
      WHEN 'AA'.
        est_fin_unl = est_fin_unl + <sfin>-size.
        lv_aa   = lv_aa + <sfin>-record_count.
        lv_faat = lv_faat + <sfin>-size.
      WHEN 'FAAT'.
        est_fin_unl = est_fin_unl + <sfin>-size.
        lv_faat = lv_faat + <sfin>-size.
      WHEN 'FI-SL'.
        est_sl  = est_sl  + <sfin>-size.
    ENDCASE.
  ENDLOOP.
  est_sfincoldch = est_sfincold * 20 / 100 + est_sfin_inv.

  IF do_sfin = abap_true.
    READ TABLE gt_sfin2 INTO ls_bseg WITH KEY table_name = 'BSEG'.
    READ TABLE gt_sfin2 INTO ls_coep WITH KEY table_name = 'COEP'.
    IF ls_bseg-record_count > 0 OR ls_coep-record_count > 0.
      avg_acdoca = ( ls_bseg-size + ls_coep-size ) / ( ls_bseg-record_count +  ls_coep-record_count ) * 75 / 100.
    ENDIF.
    "Largest # FI/NewGL/COEP WRTTP 04 + ANEA + ANEP + ANLC
    IF ls_bseg-record_count > lv_newgl.
      IF ls_coep-spec_count > ls_bseg-record_count.
        ls_sfin2-record_count = lv_aa + ls_coep-spec_count. "AA+COEP
      ELSE.
        ls_sfin2-record_count = lv_aa + ls_bseg-record_count. "AA+BSEG
      ENDIF.
    ELSE.
      IF lv_newgl > ls_coep-spec_count.
        ls_sfin2-record_count = lv_aa + lv_newgl. "AA+NewGL
      ELSE.
        ls_sfin2-record_count = lv_aa + ls_coep-spec_count. "AA+COEP
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.
    ls_sfin2-ssize      = avg_acdoca * ls_sfin2-record_count.
    ls_sfin2-table_name = 'ACDOCA'.
    ls_sfin2-group      = 'Lower estimation'.               "#EC NOTEXT
    APPEND ls_sfin2 TO gt_sfin2.
    CLEAR ls_sfin2.

    "Largest # FI/NewGL + ANEA + ANEP + ANLC + COEP WRTTP 04
    IF ls_bseg-record_count > lv_newgl.
      ls_sfin2-record_count = lv_aa + ls_coep-spec_count + ls_bseg-record_count. "AA+COEP+BSEG
    ELSE.
      ls_sfin2-record_count = lv_aa + ls_coep-spec_count + lv_newgl.
      "AA+COEP+NEWGL
    ENDIF.
    ls_sfin2-table_name = 'ACDOCA'.
    ls_sfin2-group      = 'Upper estimation'.               "#EC NOTEXT
    ls_sfin2-ssize      = avg_acdoca * ls_sfin2-record_count.
    PERFORM add2gt_tables USING ls_sfin2.
    APPEND ls_sfin2 TO gt_sfin2.
    CLEAR ls_sfin2.

    ls_sfin2-table_name = 'FAAT_DOC_IT'.
    ls_sfin2-group      = 'FI-AA'.
    ls_sfin2-ssize      = lv_faat * 15 / 100.
    PERFORM add2gt_tables USING ls_sfin2.
    APPEND ls_sfin2 TO gt_sfin2.
    CLEAR ls_sfin2.
    ls_sfin2-table_name = 'FAAT_PLAN_VALUES'.
    ls_sfin2-group      = 'FI-AA'.
    ls_sfin2-ssize      = lv_faat * 25 / 100.
    PERFORM add2gt_tables USING ls_sfin2.
    APPEND ls_sfin2 TO gt_sfin2.
    CLEAR ls_sfin2.
    ls_sfin2-table_name = 'FAAT_YDDA'.
    ls_sfin2-group      = 'FI-AA'.
    ls_sfin2-ssize      = lv_faat * 10 / 100.
    PERFORM add2gt_tables USING ls_sfin2.
    APPEND ls_sfin2 TO gt_sfin2.
    CLEAR ls_sfin2.

    LOOP AT gt_sfin2 ASSIGNING <sfin> WHERE group = 'FI-AA' OR group = 'Upper estimation'. "#EC NOTEXT
      est_sfintab = est_sfintab + <sfin>-ssize.
    ENDLOOP.

    READ TABLE gt_sfin2 ASSIGNING <sfin> WITH KEY table_name = 'BSEG'.
    IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
      <sfin>-ssize = <sfin>-size * 13 / 100.
      est_sfincol = est_sfincol + <sfin>-ssize.
      READ TABLE gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WITH KEY table_name = <sfin>-table_name BINARY SEARCH.
      IF sy-dbsys(3) = 'HDB'.
        <item>-real_size = <item>-real_size + <sfin>-ssize.
      ELSE.
        <item>-est_size  = <item>-est_size  + <sfin>-ssize.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.
  ENDIF.

  READ TABLE gt_sfin2 ASSIGNING <sfin> WITH KEY table_name = 'COEP'.
  IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
    IF do_sfin = abap_true.
      <sfin>-ssize = <sfin>-size * 15 / 100.
      est_sfincol = est_sfincol + <sfin>-ssize.
      READ TABLE gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WITH KEY table_name = <sfin>-table_name BINARY SEARCH.
      IF sy-dbsys(3) = 'HDB'.
        <item>-real_size = <item>-real_size + <sfin>-ssize.
      ELSE.
        <item>-est_size  = <item>-est_size  + <sfin>-ssize.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.
    actual_ratio = <sfin>-spec_count / <sfin>-record_count.
    <sfin>-osize = ( <sfin>-size + <sfin>-ssize ) * actual_ratio.
    est_delcoep = est_delcoep + <sfin>-osize.
    LOOP AT gt_sfin2 ASSIGNING <sfin> WHERE group = 'OBSCO'.
      <sfin>-osize = <sfin>-size * actual_ratio.
      est_delcoep = est_delcoep + <sfin>-osize.
    ENDLOOP.
  ENDIF.

  SORT gt_sfin2 BY size DESCENDING.
ENDFORM.                    "sfin_sizing

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  EC_PCA_SIZING
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM ec_pca_sizing.
  DATA ls_ec_pca TYPE ty_ssol.
  LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WHERE store = 'CS'.
    CASE <item>-table_name.
      WHEN 'GLPCA' OR 'GLPCC' OR 'GLPCO' OR 'GLPCP' OR 'GLPCT'.
        ls_ec_pca-group = 'EC-PCA'.
        MOVE-CORRESPONDING <item> TO ls_ec_pca.
        IF sy-dbsys(3) = 'HDB'.
          ls_ec_pca-size = <item>-real_size.
        ELSE.
          ls_ec_pca-size = <item>-est_size.
        ENDIF.
        INSERT ls_ec_pca INTO TABLE gt_ec_pca.
        CLEAR ls_ec_pca.
        ADD ls_ec_pca-size TO est_pca.
    ENDCASE.
  ENDLOOP.
  SORT gt_ec_pca BY size DESCENDING.
ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  ADD2GT_TABLES
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       add new data model tables to tables list
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*

FORM add2gt_tables USING ls_snew TYPE ty_ssol.
  READ TABLE gt_tables WITH KEY table_name = ls_snew-table_name TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS BINARY SEARCH.
  tabix = sy-tabix.
  IF sy-subrc IS NOT INITIAL.
    CLEAR table_item.
    MOVE-CORRESPONDING ls_snew TO table_item.
    table_item-db_table = ls_snew-table_name.
    table_item-part_id  = 1.
    table_item-tab_type = 'TRANSP'.
    table_item-store    = 'CS'.
    table_item-clitab   = abap_true.
    " Do not add to subtotal as this is later added
    IF sy-dbsys(3) = 'HDB'.
      table_item-real_size = ls_snew-ssize.
    ELSE.
      table_item-est_size  = ls_snew-ssize.
    ENDIF.
    INSERT table_item INTO gt_tables INDEX tabix.
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    "add2gt_tables

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  UPD_OPT_SIZE
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       update optimal size in gt_tables
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*

FORM upd_opt_size.

  LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item>.
    "delete non-unique indexes
    IF sy-dbsys(3) = 'HDB'.
      <item>-opt_size = <item>-real_size - <item>-real_nuk_size.
    ELSE.
      <item>-opt_size = <item>-est_size - <item>-est_nuk_size.
      IF <item>-opt_pageable_size > 0.
        <item>-opt_pageable_size = <item>-opt_pageable_size - <item>-est_nuk_size.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.
    "simple finance changes
    READ TABLE gt_sfin2 ASSIGNING <sfin>
      WITH KEY table_name = <item>-table_name.
    IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
      CASE <sfin>-group.
        WHEN 'NEWCOL'. "=> already added at migration
*          <item>-opt_size = <item>-opt_size + <sfin>-ssize.
          IF <item>-table_name = 'COEP'.
            <item>-opt_size = <item>-opt_size - <sfin>-osize.
          ENDIF.
        WHEN 'OBSCO'.
          <item>-opt_size = <item>-opt_size - <sfin>-osize.
        WHEN 'FI-AA'.
        WHEN OTHERS.
          IF <item>-table_name <> 'ACDOCA'.
            CLEAR <item>-opt_size.
          ENDIF.
      ENDCASE.
    ENDIF.
    "simple logistics changes
    READ TABLE gt_slog ASSIGNING <slog>
      WITH KEY table_name = <item>-table_name.
    IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
      CASE <slog>-group.
        WHEN 'NEWCOL'. "=> already added at migration
*          <item>-opt_size = <item>-opt_size + <slog>-ssize.
        WHEN 'VBFA' OR 'TAB'.
        WHEN OTHERS.
          CLEAR <item>-opt_size.
      ENDCASE.
    ENDIF.

    "nse. Calculate the memory usage of table if use NSE
    IF <item>-opt_pageable_size > 0.
      "opt is unpageable part (Cache is counted separately)
      IF sy-dbsys(3) = 'HDB'.
        <item>-opt_size = <item>-real_size - <item>-opt_pageable_size.
      ELSE.
        <item>-opt_size = <item>-est_size - <item>-opt_pageable_size.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.

    "ml
    READ TABLE gt_ml ASSIGNING <ml> WITH KEY table_name = <item>-table_name.
    IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
      IF <ml>-group = 'OBS'.
        CLEAR <item>-opt_size.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.

    "soh to S4 sizing (LRAW to HL)
    READ TABLE gt_soh2s4 ASSIGNING <soh2s4> WITH KEY table_name = <item>-table_name reason = 'LRAW2HL' BINARY SEARCH.
    IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
      <item>-opt_size = <soh2s4>-opt_size.
      "Calculate subtotals (not possible earlier as real_size not yet
      "calculated
      <soh2s4>-soh_size = <item>-real_size.
      est_lraw2hl_gain = est_lraw2hl_gain +  <soh2s4>-soh_size - <soh2s4>-opt_size.
      est_lraw2hl_hl_growth = est_lraw2hl_hl_growth + <soh2s4>-opt_hl_size.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.
ENDFORM.                    "upd_opt_size

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  SEARCH_HIGH_CARD
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       Search for the column with high cardinality
*       This routine might not find it
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*

FORM search_high_card USING lt_keyfields TYPE ty_t_keyfields
                            keycount     TYPE i.

  DATA floating_number TYPE f.
  FIELD-SYMBOLS <key> TYPE ty_keyfields.

  DEFINE mc_size_u.
    if <item>-record_count > 0.
      <cs_size>-est_ms_dict = <cs_size>-opt_size_byte * <item>-record_count / idx_dict_comp.
      floating_number = <item>-record_count * log( <item>-record_count ) / log( 2 ) / 8.
      <cs_size>-est_ms_data  = floating_number.
    endif.
    <cs_size>-est_ms_index = <cs_size>-est_ms_data.
    <cs_size>-est_ms_misc  = size_in_misc_default.
    <cs_size>-est_ms_main  = <cs_size>-est_ms_data
                           + <cs_size>-est_ms_dict
                           + <cs_size>-est_ms_index
                           + <cs_size>-est_ms_misc.
  END-OF-DEFINITION.

  IF keycount = 1. "one field key.
    mc_size_u.
    <cs_size>-has_index = 'U'.
  ENDIF.
  IF keycount = 2.
    "2 fields in the key and 1 is client.
    READ TABLE lt_keyfields TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS WITH KEY client = abap_true.
    IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
      READ TABLE lt_keyfields ASSIGNING <key> WITH KEY client = abap_false.
      IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL."case if all fields are of type mandt.
        READ TABLE <item>-cs_cols ASSIGNING <cs_size> WITH KEY column_name = <key>-column_name.
        mc_size_u.
        <cs_size>-has_index = 'U'.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.
  ENDIF.
  IF keycount > 2.
    "Search for GUIDs fields
    LOOP AT lt_keyfields ASSIGNING <key>.
      IF <key>-typekind = cl_abap_typedescr=>typekind_hex.
        READ TABLE <item>-cs_cols ASSIGNING <cs_size> WITH KEY column_name = <key>-column_name.
        IF <cs_size>-has_index <> 'U'.
          mc_size_u.
          <cs_size>-has_index = 'G'.
        ENDIF.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    "search_high_card

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form fill_inplace_list
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       collect list of cloned tables
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*

FORM fill_inplace_list USING lt_inplace TYPE ty_t_upgrade.
  DATA: ls_inplace TYPE ty_upgrade,
        l_len      TYPE i.
  CONSTANTS newgl_t800a TYPE tabname VALUE 't800a'.         "#EC NOTEXT

  DEFINE mc_add_inplace.
    READ TABLE gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WITH KEY table_name = &1 BINARY SEARCH.
    IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
      ls_inplace-table_name = <item>-table_name.
      IF sy-dbsys(3) = 'HDB'.
        ls_inplace-size     = <item>-real_size.
        ls_inplace-pksize   = <item>-real_pk_size.
        ls_inplace-disksize = <item>-real_size + <item>-real_hl_size.
      ELSE.
        ls_inplace-size     = <item>-est_size.
        ls_inplace-pksize   = <item>-est_pk_size.
        ls_inplace-disksize = <item>-est_size + <item>-est_hl_size.
      ENDIF.
      ls_inplace-record_count = <item>-record_count.
      APPEND ls_inplace TO lt_inplace.
    ENDIF.
  END-OF-DEFINITION.

  IF in_sfin = abap_false.
    TRY.
        SELECT DISTINCT tab FROM (newgl_t800a) INTO ls_inplace-table_name
          WHERE appl = 'FI' AND glflex = 'X' AND inactive = space
            AND ( subappl = 'GLF' OR subappl = 'PSM' OR subappl = 'PSX' OR subappl = 'JVA' ).
          mc_add_inplace ls_inplace-table_name.
        ENDSELECT.
      CATCH cx_sy_dynamic_osql_semantics. "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.
    SELECT tabname FROM dd02l INTO ls_inplace-table_name WHERE as4local = 'A' AND tabname LIKE 'CE4%'.
      l_len = strlen( ls_inplace-table_name ).
      IF l_len = 7.
        mc_add_inplace ls_inplace-table_name.
      ENDIF.
    ENDSELECT.
  ENDIF.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  fill_shadow_list
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       fill list of tables cloned to shadow instance.
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*

FORM fill_shadow_list USING lt_shadow TYPE ty_t_upgrade.
  DATA ls_shadow TYPE ty_upgrade.

  DEFINE mc_add.
    ls_shadow-table_name = &1.
    READ TABLE gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WITH KEY table_name = ls_shadow-table_name BINARY SEARCH.
    IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
      IF sy-dbsys(3) = 'HDB'.
        ls_shadow-size     = <item>-real_size.
        ls_shadow-pksize   = <item>-real_pk_size.
        ls_shadow-disksize = <item>-real_size + <item>-real_hl_size.
      ELSE.
        ls_shadow-size     = <item>-est_size.
        ls_shadow-pksize   = <item>-est_pk_size.
        ls_shadow-disksize = <item>-est_size + <item>-est_hl_size.
      ENDIF.
      ls_shadow-record_count = <item>-record_count.
      APPEND ls_shadow TO lt_shadow.
    ENDIF.
  END-OF-DEFINITION.

  mc_add '/1BS/TEST_T_FK'. mc_add '/1BS/TEST_TABLE'.
  mc_add '/BOBF/ACF_MAP'. mc_add '/BOBF/ACT_CONF'.
  mc_add '/BOBF/ACT_LIST'. mc_add '/BOBF/ACT_LISTT'.

ENDFORM.                    "fill_shadow_list

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  get_anydb_size
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       Get used size on disk of analysed database in bytes
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM get_anydb_size CHANGING anydbsize     TYPE numeric "bytes
                             anydbsizedate TYPE sydats.
  DATA: td110         TYPE td110_stru,
        lt_db6pmdb02  TYPE TABLE OF db6pmdb02,
        ls_db6pmdb02  TYPE db6pmdb02,
        db4size       TYPE db4size,
        l_db_sizeinfo TYPE mssdbsizeinfo,
        size_mb       TYPE i,
        ls_stats      TYPE ada_devsta,
        lt_stats      TYPE TABLE OF ada_devsta,
        lt_sp_hist    TYPE TABLE OF ada_dbhist,
        mindate       TYPE d.

  MESSAGE 'Read analysed db disk size' TYPE 'S'.            "#EC NOTEXT
  TRY.
      CASE sy-dbsys(3).
        WHEN 'MSS'.
          CALL FUNCTION 'MSS_GET_DB_SIZE_INFO'
            IMPORTING
              db_sizeinfo          = l_db_sizeinfo "mb
            EXCEPTIONS
              not_running_on_mssql = 1
              db_error             = 2
              internal_error       = 3
              db_not_found         = 4
              no_db_access         = 5
              OTHERS               = 6.
          IF sy-subrc IS NOT INITIAL.
            RETURN.
          ENDIF.
          anydbsize = l_db_sizeinfo-db_alloc.
          mb2b anydbsize. "bytes
        WHEN 'DB2'.
          TRY.
              CALL FUNCTION 'DB2_KPI_DB_USED_SPACE' "mb
                IMPORTING
                  used_space = size_mb.
              anydbsize = size_mb.
              mb2b anydbsize. "bytes
            CATCH cx_sy_dyn_call_illegal_func.
              RETURN.
          ENDTRY.
        WHEN 'ORA'.
          CALL FUNCTION 'DB02_ORA_FILL_TD110'
            IMPORTING
              td110 = td110. "kb.
          mindate = sy-datum - 30.
          IF td110-datum < mindate AND sy-batch = abap_true.
            TRY.
                CALL FUNCTION 'DB02_ORA_FILL_TD110'
                  EXPORTING
                    flag_refresh = 'Y'
                  IMPORTING
                    td110        = td110. "kb
              CATCH cx_root. "#EC NO_HANDLER
            ENDTRY.
          ENDIF.
          anydbsizedate = td110-datum.
          anydbsize = td110-tssi - td110-tsfr.
          anydbsize = anydbsize * 1024. "bytes
          anydbsizedate = td110-datum.
        WHEN 'SYB'.
          TRY.
              CALL FUNCTION 'SYB_DB_SIZE'
                IMPORTING
                  reserved_size         = size_mb
                EXCEPTIONS
                  invalid_parameter_set = 1
                  adbc_error            = 2
                  system_error          = 3
                  OTHERS                = 4.
              IF sy-subrc IS NOT INITIAL.
                RETURN.
              ENDIF.
              anydbsize = size_mb.
              mb2b anydbsize. "bytes
            CATCH cx_sy_dyn_call_illegal_func.
              RETURN.
          ENDTRY.
        WHEN 'ADA'.
          CALL FUNCTION 'ADA_DB_FILLING'
            TABLES
              devstat                        = lt_stats "kb
              devsp_hist                     = lt_sp_hist
            EXCEPTIONS
              table_not_found_versions       = 1
              table_not_found_dbparameters   = 2
              table_not_found_serverdbstatis = 3
              no_entry_found_versions        = 4
              no_entry_found_dbparameters    = 5
              no_entry_found_serverdbstatist = 6
              error_get_db_info_ada          = 7
              error_sel_serverdbstat_ada     = 8
              error_sel_dbparameters_ada     = 9
              OTHERS                         = 10.
          IF sy-subrc IS NOT INITIAL.
            RETURN.
          ENDIF.
          READ TABLE lt_stats INTO ls_stats INDEX 1.
          anydbsize = ls_stats-perm_used * 1024.
        WHEN 'INF'.
        WHEN 'DB4'.
          CALL FUNCTION 'GET_DB4_DBSIZE'
            IMPORTING
              db4_dbsize                    = db4size "kb
            EXCEPTIONS
              wrong_dbsys                   = 1
              dbstattdb4_empty              = 2
              api_qwcrssts_error            = 3
              dbstat_empty_api_error        = 4
              import_from_moni_error        = 5
              dbstat_empty_moni_error       = 6
              api_error_moni_error          = 7
              dbstat_empty_api_err_moni_err = 8
              consistency_check_error       = 9
              api_error                     = 10
              OTHERS                        = 11.
          IF sy-subrc IS NOT INITIAL.
            RETURN.
          ENDIF.
          anydbsize = db4size-db_size.
          anydbsize = anydbsize * 1024.
        WHEN 'DB6'.
          CALL FUNCTION 'DB6_HIS_OVERVIEW'
            TABLES
              it_db6pmdb02     = lt_db6pmdb02 "kb
            EXCEPTIONS
              no_history_found = 1
              OTHERS           = 2.
          IF sy-subrc IS NOT INITIAL.
            RETURN.
          ELSE.
            READ TABLE lt_db6pmdb02 INTO ls_db6pmdb02 INDEX 1.
          ENDIF.
          anydbsize = ls_db6pmdb02-totalkb - ls_db6pmdb02-freekb.
          anydbsize = anydbsize * 1024.
        WHEN 'HDB'.
          EXEC SQL.
            select sum(used_size) into :anydbsize from M_DATA_VOLUME_STATISTICS
          ENDEXEC.                                      "#EC CI_EXECSQL
      ENDCASE.
    CATCH cx_sy_dyn_call_illegal_func
          cx_root.
      CLEAR anydbsize.
  ENDTRY.

ENDFORM.                    "get_anydb_size

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  calculate_subtotals_calib
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       Calculate detailed sub totals.
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM calculate_subtotals_calib.

  ls_cs_cal-column_name = 'trexexternalkey'.                "#EC NOTEXT
  APPEND ls_cs_cal TO lt_cs_cal. "1
  ls_cs_cal-column_name = 'rowid'.                          "#EC NOTEXT
  APPEND ls_cs_cal TO lt_cs_cal. "2
  ls_cs_cal-column_name = 'trex_udiv'.                      "#EC NOTEXT
  APPEND ls_cs_cal TO lt_cs_cal. "3
  ls_cs_cal-column_name = 'Unique indexes'.                 "#EC NOTEXT
  APPEND ls_cs_cal TO lt_cs_cal.  "4
  ls_cs_cal-column_name = 'Entreprise Search'.              "#EC NOTEXT
  APPEND ls_cs_cal TO lt_cs_cal. "5
  ls_cs_cal-column_name = 'Concatenated JE indexes'.        "#EC NOTEXT
  APPEND ls_cs_cal TO lt_cs_cal. "6
  ls_cs_cal-column_name = 'LOB Columns'.                    "#EC NOTEXT
  APPEND ls_cs_cal TO lt_cs_cal. "7
  ls_cs_cal-column_name = 'Hybrid LOB Columns'.             "#EC NOTEXT
  APPEND ls_cs_cal TO lt_cs_cal. "8
  ls_cs_cal-column_name = 'U Columns'.                      "#EC NOTEXT
  APPEND ls_cs_cal TO lt_cs_cal. "9
  ls_cs_cal-column_name = 'N Columns'.                      "#EC NOTEXT
  APPEND ls_cs_cal TO lt_cs_cal. "10
  ls_cs_cal-column_name = 'P Columns'.                      "#EC NOTEXT
  APPEND ls_cs_cal TO lt_cs_cal. "11
  ls_cs_cal-column_name = 'Low opt. Columns'.               "#EC NOTEXT
  APPEND ls_cs_cal TO lt_cs_cal. "12
  ls_cs_cal-column_name = 'Other Columns'.                  "#EC NOTEXT
  APPEND ls_cs_cal TO lt_cs_cal. "13

  LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item>.
    IF <item>-store = 'CS'.
      LOOP AT <item>-cs_cols ASSIGNING <cs_size>.
        CASE <cs_size>-column_name.
          WHEN '$trexexternalkey$'.
            READ TABLE lt_cs_cal ASSIGNING <cscal> INDEX 1.
          WHEN '$rowid$'.
            READ TABLE lt_cs_cal ASSIGNING <cscal> INDEX 2.
          WHEN '$trex_udiv$'.
            READ TABLE lt_cs_cal ASSIGNING <cscal> INDEX 3.
          WHEN OTHERS.
            IF <cs_size>-column_name(3) = '$uc_'.
              READ TABLE lt_cs_cal ASSIGNING <cscal> INDEX 4.
            ELSEIF <cs_size>-column_name(13) = '$_SYS_SHADOW_' OR <cs_size>-column_name(5) = '$esh:'.
              READ TABLE lt_cs_cal ASSIGNING <cscal> INDEX 5.
            ELSE.
              IF <cs_size>-column_name(1) = '$'.
                READ TABLE lt_cs_cal ASSIGNING <cscal> INDEX 6.
              ENDIF.
              IF <cs_size>-lob_size_byte > 0.
                IF <cs_size>-dlob_count = 0.
                  READ TABLE lt_cs_cal ASSIGNING <cscal> INDEX 7.
                ELSE.
                  READ TABLE lt_cs_cal ASSIGNING <cscal> INDEX 8.
                ENDIF.
              ELSE.
                CASE <cs_size>-has_index.
                  WHEN 'U'.
                    READ TABLE lt_cs_cal ASSIGNING <cscal> INDEX 9.
                  WHEN 'N'.
                    READ TABLE lt_cs_cal ASSIGNING <cscal> INDEX 10.
                  WHEN 'P'.
                    READ TABLE lt_cs_cal ASSIGNING <cscal> INDEX 11.
                  WHEN OTHERS.
                    IF <cs_size>-opt_size_byte = 0.
                      READ TABLE lt_cs_cal ASSIGNING <cscal> INDEX 12.
                    ELSE.
                      READ TABLE lt_cs_cal ASSIGNING <cscal> INDEX 13.
                    ENDIF.
                ENDCASE.
              ENDIF.
            ENDIF.
        ENDCASE.
        <cscal>-est_ms_main  = <cscal>-est_ms_main  + <cs_size>-est_ms_main.
        <cscal>-est_ms_dict  = <cscal>-est_ms_dict  + <cs_size>-est_ms_dict.
        <cscal>-est_ms_data  = <cscal>-est_ms_data  + <cs_size>-est_ms_data.
        <cscal>-est_ms_index = <cscal>-est_ms_index + <cs_size>-est_ms_index.
        <cscal>-est_ms_misc  = <cscal>-est_ms_misc  + <cs_size>-est_ms_misc.
        <cscal>-ms_main  = <cscal>-ms_main  + <cs_size>-ms_main.
        <cscal>-ms_dict  = <cscal>-ms_dict  + <cs_size>-ms_dict.
        <cscal>-ms_data  = <cscal>-ms_data  + <cs_size>-ms_data.
        <cscal>-ms_index = <cscal>-ms_index + <cs_size>-ms_index.
        <cscal>-ms_misc  = <cscal>-ms_misc  + <cs_size>-ms_misc.
      ENDLOOP.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.                    "calculate_subtotals_calib

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& FORM  collect_stats
*& Control the RFC calls, packaging and parallelism
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*

FORM collect_stats USING mode TYPE string.
  DATA: nb_tables TYPE i,
        l_count   TYPE p DECIMALS 2.

  DESCRIBE TABLE gt_input LINES nb_tables.
  " Adapt parallel if bigger than # of tables.
  IF nb_tables < p_paral.
    p_paral = nb_tables.
  ENDIF.
  "Adapt bucket size if small selection of tables
  IF bucket_size > nb_tables.
    bucket_size =  nb_tables / p_paral + 1.
  ENDIF.
  " Create buckets. Cluster/pool tables must be grouped in the same.
  LOOP AT gt_input ASSIGNING <item>.
    IF p_db_table <> <item>-db_table.
      p_db_table = <item>-db_table.
      ADD 1 TO l_count.
    ENDIF.
    <item>-bucket = l_count DIV bucket_size.
  ENDLOOP.
  nb_buckets = <item>-bucket + 1.
  CLEAR p_db_table.

  " call one RFC per bucket
  CONCATENATE '1ST' mode INTO mode.
  LOOP AT gt_input ASSIGNING <item>.
    IF <item>-bucket <> bucket.
      PERFORM do_rfc TABLES gt_bucket
                      USING bucket
                            wa_techd-prec
                            mode.
      bucket = <item>-bucket.
      CALL FUNCTION 'DB_COMMIT'.
      WAIT UNTIL l_act < p_paral.
      CLEAR gt_bucket.
    ENDIF.
    APPEND <item> TO gt_bucket.
  ENDLOOP.

  " perform last call.
  CALL FUNCTION 'DB_COMMIT'.
  WAIT UNTIL l_act < p_paral.
  PERFORM do_rfc TABLES gt_bucket
                  USING bucket
                        wa_techd-prec
                        mode.
  CALL FUNCTION 'DB_COMMIT'.
  WAIT UNTIL l_sent = l_recvd.

  CLEAR: gt_bucket, l_act, l_recvd, l_sent, bucket.

  " retry erroneous in single RFC.
  IF lt_retry IS NOT INITIAL.
    CONCATENATE 'RET' mode+3 INTO mode.
    MESSAGE 'Warning: Error encountered. Check ST22.' TYPE 'S'. "#EC NOTEXT
    DESCRIBE TABLE lt_retry LINES l_retrycnt.
    MESSAGE 'Reprocessing of erroneous calls started' TYPE 'S'. "#EC NOTEXT
    LOOP AT lt_retry ASSIGNING <item>.
      IF p_db_table <> <item>-db_table AND p_db_table IS NOT INITIAL.
        PERFORM do_rfc TABLES gt_bucket
                        USING bucket
                              wa_techd-prec
                              mode.
        CALL FUNCTION 'DB_COMMIT'.
        WAIT UNTIL l_act < p_paral.
        CLEAR gt_bucket.
      ENDIF.
      p_db_table = <item>-db_table.
      APPEND <item> TO gt_bucket.
    ENDLOOP.

    " perform last call.
    CALL FUNCTION 'DB_COMMIT'.
    WAIT UNTIL l_act < p_paral.
    PERFORM do_rfc TABLES gt_bucket
                    USING bucket
                          wa_techd-prec
                          mode.
    CALL FUNCTION 'DB_COMMIT'.
    WAIT UNTIL l_sent = l_recvd.
    MESSAGE 'Reprocessing of erroneous calls finished' TYPE 'S'. "#EC NOTEXT
  ENDIF.
  CLEAR nb_buckets.
  REFRESH: gt_input, gt_bucket, lt_retry.
  SORT gt_tables BY table_name.
  SORT gt_columns BY table_name column_name.
  MESSAGE 'End of statistics collection' TYPE 'S'.          "#EC NOTEXT
ENDFORM.                    "collect_stats

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  changes_s4
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       Estimates potential size changes if system is already HANA
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM changes_s4.
  TYPES: BEGIN OF ty_lraw_tabs,
           tabname   TYPE tabname,
           fieldname TYPE fieldname,
         END OF ty_lraw_tabs.
  DATA:
    lt_s4changes2size TYPE ty_t_hana_db_size,
    ls_s4changes2size TYPE ty_hana_db_size,
    lt_lraw_tabs      TYPE TABLE OF ty_lraw_tabs,
    ls_soh2s4         TYPE ty_soh2s4.
  FIELD-SYMBOLS:
    <s4ch_col> TYPE ty_cs_size,
    <lraw>     TYPE ty_lraw_tabs,
    <s4chg>    TYPE ty_hana_db_size.

  "Until a larger code redesign is done, we need to remove the entries
  "from gt_tables and later add them back.

  "Find tables that are in RS but will be moved to CS
  PERFORM fill_row_list.
  LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WHERE store = 'RS'.
    tabix = sy-tabix.
    READ TABLE gt_rownots4_tab WITH KEY table_line = <item>-table_name TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS BINARY SEARCH.
    IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
      CLEAR <item>-bucket.
      APPEND <item> TO gt_input.
      ls_soh2s4-table_name = <item>-table_name.
      ls_soh2s4-reason     = 'RS2CS'.
      "as the conversion happens during the upgrade,
      "keep track of current size for later display.
      LOOP AT <item>-rs_cols ASSIGNING <rs_size>.
        ls_soh2s4-soh_size = ls_soh2s4-soh_size + <rs_size>-fixed_size + <rs_size>-variable_size.
      ENDLOOP.
      APPEND ls_soh2s4 TO gt_soh2s4.
      CLEAR ls_soh2s4.
      DELETE gt_tables INDEX tabix.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.
  SORT gt_tables BY table_name.

  "find tables with LRAW, not using yet LOB (only CS)
  SELECT tabname fieldname FROM dd03l INTO TABLE lt_lraw_tabs
    WHERE as4local = 'A' AND datatype = 'LRAW' AND tabname IN so_tab AND leng BETWEEN '1000' AND '5000'.

  LOOP AT lt_lraw_tabs ASSIGNING <lraw>.
    READ TABLE gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WITH KEY table_name = <lraw>-tabname BINARY SEARCH.
    tabix = sy-tabix.
    IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL AND <item>-cs_cols IS NOT INITIAL AND <item>-record_count > 10000.
      READ TABLE <item>-cs_cols ASSIGNING <cs_size> WITH KEY column_name = <lraw>-fieldname.
      IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL AND <cs_size>-ms_hl = 0 AND <item>-load_unit <> 'PAGE'.
        READ TABLE gt_nse_list WITH KEY table_name = <lraw>-tabname BINARY SEARCH TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS.
        IF sy-subrc IS NOT INITIAL.
          "column is not using HL yet, is not in NSE, and will not be in NSE
          CLEAR <item>-bucket.
          APPEND <item> TO gt_input.
          ls_soh2s4-table_name = <item>-table_name.
          ls_soh2s4-reason     = 'LRAW2HL'.
          APPEND ls_soh2s4 TO gt_soh2s4.
          CLEAR ls_soh2s4.
          DELETE gt_tables INDEX tabix.
        ENDIF.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.
  SORT gt_tables BY table_name.

  IF gt_input IS NOT INITIAL.
    "Not possible yet but for future proofing
    SORT gt_input BY table_name.
    DELETE ADJACENT DUPLICATES FROM gt_input COMPARING table_name.

    "collect statistics
    MESSAGE 'Statistics collection for S4 changes' TYPE 'S'. "#EC NOTEXT
    mode = 'CAL'.
    PERFORM collect_stats USING mode.
    "CAL mode returns HANA size in <item>-*size
    "And row size estimations in gt_columns

    "Build sizing input table
    LOOP AT gt_soh2s4 ASSIGNING <soh2s4>.
      READ TABLE gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WITH KEY table_name = <soh2s4>-table_name BINARY SEARCH.
      MOVE <item> TO ls_s4changes2size.
      CLEAR: ls_s4changes2size-cs_cols, ls_s4changes2size-rs_cols.
      LOOP AT gt_columns ASSIGNING <columns> WHERE table_name = <soh2s4>-table_name.
        MOVE-CORRESPONDING <columns> TO gs_cs_size.
        APPEND gs_cs_size TO ls_s4changes2size-cs_cols.
        CLEAR gs_cs_size.
      ENDLOOP.
      IF <soh2s4>-reason = 'RS2CS'.
        ls_s4changes2size-store = 'CS'.
      ENDIF.
      APPEND ls_s4changes2size TO lt_s4changes2size.
      CLEAR ls_s4changes2size.
    ENDLOOP.
    FREE: gs_cs_size, gt_columns.

    "Perform the estimations
    PERFORM sizing_calculation CHANGING lt_s4changes2size.

    "Merge the results into gt_s4opt
    LOOP AT lt_s4changes2size ASSIGNING <s4chg>.
      READ TABLE gt_soh2s4 WITH KEY table_name = <s4chg>-table_name ASSIGNING <soh2s4>.
      READ TABLE gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WITH KEY table_name = <s4chg>-table_name BINARY SEARCH.

      IF <soh2s4>-reason = 'LRAW2HL'.
        "Loop on <item>-cs_cols to make sure we take all existing columns
        "instead of relying on estimated list of columns
        LOOP AT <item>-cs_cols ASSIGNING <cs_size>.
          "Check if table has LRAW and is changed
          READ TABLE lt_lraw_tabs ASSIGNING <lraw> WITH KEY tabname   = <item>-table_name
                                                            fieldname = <cs_size>-column_name.
          IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
            "use the column estimated size from sizing_calculation
            "Only if HL will be used.
            READ TABLE <s4chg>-cs_cols ASSIGNING <s4ch_col> WITH KEY column_name = <cs_size>-column_name.
            IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL AND <s4ch_col>-dlob_count > 0.
              <soh2s4>-opt_size    = <soh2s4>-opt_size    + <s4ch_col>-est_ms_main.
              <soh2s4>-opt_hl_size = <soh2s4>-opt_hl_size + <s4ch_col>-est_ms_hl.
            ELSE.
              "LOB are too small and stay in memory. Use the actual size
              <soh2s4>-opt_size    = <soh2s4>-opt_size    + <cs_size>-ms_main.
              <soh2s4>-opt_hl_size = <soh2s4>-opt_hl_size + <cs_size>-ms_hl.
            ENDIF.
          ELSE.
            "Not an LRAW field. Use the actual size
            <soh2s4>-opt_size    = <soh2s4>-opt_size    + <cs_size>-ms_main.
            <soh2s4>-opt_hl_size = <soh2s4>-opt_hl_size + <cs_size>-ms_hl.
          ENDIF.
        ENDLOOP.
      ENDIF.
      IF <soh2s4>-reason = 'RS2CS'.
        "We must use estimated size of columns
        LOOP AT <s4chg>-cs_cols ASSIGNING <s4ch_col>.
          <soh2s4>-opt_size    = <soh2s4>-opt_size    + <s4ch_col>-est_ms_main.
          <soh2s4>-opt_hl_size = <soh2s4>-opt_hl_size + <s4ch_col>-est_ms_hl.
        ENDLOOP.
        "Move est. to real. Later code will see this table as CS.
        <item>-store = 'CS'.
        <item>-cs_cols = <s4chg>-cs_cols.
        CLEAR <item>-rs_cols.
        LOOP AT <item>-cs_cols ASSIGNING <cs_size>.
          <cs_size>-ms_main  = <cs_size>-est_ms_main.
          <cs_size>-ms_dict  = <cs_size>-est_ms_dict.
          <cs_size>-ms_index = <cs_size>-est_ms_index.
          <cs_size>-ms_data  = <cs_size>-est_ms_data.
          <cs_size>-ms_misc  = <cs_size>-est_ms_misc.
          <cs_size>-ms_hl    = <cs_size>-est_ms_hl.
        ENDLOOP.
        "update subtotals
        "1.Growth of Column Store
        est_rs2cs_cs_growth = est_rs2cs_cs_growth + <soh2s4>-opt_size.
        est_hl_rs2cs_growth = est_hl_rs2cs_growth + <soh2s4>-opt_hl_size.
        "2.Reduction of Row Store
        est_rs2cs_rs_gain = est_rs2cs_rs_gain + <soh2s4>-soh_size.
        "Send the table to the
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.
    SORT gt_soh2s4 BY table_name.
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    "changes_s4

  mc_add_s 'FAGL_TLDGRP_MAP' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'FINS_ML_ACCOUNT' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'FINSC_CMP_VERSND' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'FINSC_LD_CMP' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'FMLT_CURTP_ML' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'KNB5' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'KNBK' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'KNKK' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'KNVP' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'KNVV' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'MARCH' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'MARD' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'MARDH' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'ONRAO' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'PRPS' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'T000' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'T006' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'T093' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'T093A' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'T093C' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'T311A' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'TCURX' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'TJ01' 'OSTR'.
  mc_add_s 'TKA01' 'OSTR'.

  IF sy-dbsys(3) = 'HDB'.
    sizefield = 'REAL_SIZE'.
  ELSE.
    sizefield = 'EST_SIZE'.
  ENDIF.

  "Sum up scale-out group sizes.
  LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item>.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT sizefield OF STRUCTURE <item> TO <sizefs>.
    READ TABLE gt_sogrp ASSIGNING <sogrp> WITH KEY group = <item>-sogroup.
    IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
      <sogrp>-size     = <sogrp>-size + <sizefs>.
      <sogrp>-opt_size = <sogrp>-opt_size + <item>-opt_size.
    ELSE.
      ls_sogrp-group    = <item>-sogroup.
      ls_sogrp-size     = <sizefs>.
      ls_sogrp-opt_size = <item>-opt_size.
      APPEND ls_sogrp TO gt_sogrp.
      CLEAR ls_sogrp.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.
  READ TABLE gt_sogrp ASSIGNING <sogrp> WITH KEY group = ''.
  IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
    <sogrp>-group = 'COL_TABLES_NOT_GROUPED'.
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                                     "calculate_scaleout_group.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  nse_sizing.
*&      Estimate gain if converted to NSE
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM nse_sizing.
  FIELD-SYMBOLS <nselist> TYPE ty_nse_table.

  IF gt_nse_list IS INITIAL.
    PERFORM fill_nse_list CHANGING gt_nse_list.
  ENDIF.

  "Calculate the pageable size
  LOOP AT gt_nse_list ASSIGNING <nselist>.
    READ TABLE gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WITH KEY table_name = <nselist>-table_name BINARY SEARCH.
    IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL AND <item>-load_unit <> 'PAGE'.
      LOOP AT <item>-cs_cols ASSIGNING <cs_size>
        WHERE column_name <> '$rowid$' AND column_name <> '$trex_udiv$' AND column_name(5) <> '$esh:'.
        "Calculate size of pageable data on table level
        <item>-opt_pageable_size = <item>-opt_pageable_size + <cs_size>-est_ms_main.
        <item>-opt_pageable_size = <item>-opt_pageable_size + <cs_size>-ms_main.
      ENDLOOP.
      "Update subtotal
      opt_pageable_data  = opt_pageable_data  + <item>-opt_pageable_size.
      opt_pageable_cache = opt_pageable_cache + ( <item>-opt_pageable_size / c_nse_ratio ).
*      "Update gt_nse
*      ls_nse-table_name = <item>-table_name.
*      ls_nse-opt_pageable_data = <item>-opt_pageable_size.
*      APPEND ls_nse TO gt_nse.
*      CLEAR ls_nse.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  get_dvm_info.
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM get_dvm_info.
  TYPE-POOLS adk.
  CONSTANTS c_admi_run(8) VALUE 'admi_run'.                 "#EC NOTEXT

  "downport to 640 from cl_adk_ccms_get_objects
  TYPES:
    BEGIN OF ty_s_object,
      object(10)      TYPE c,
      object_text(50) TYPE c,
      sign(1)         TYPE c,
      tabnames        TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF tabname WITH DEFAULT KEY,
    END OF ty_s_object,
    ty_t_objects TYPE SORTED TABLE OF ty_s_object WITH UNIQUE KEY object,
    BEGIN OF ty_s_objects_for_table,
      tabname TYPE tabname,
      objects TYPE ty_t_objects,
    END OF ty_s_objects_for_table,
    ty_t_objects_for_tables TYPE SORTED TABLE OF ty_s_objects_for_table WITH UNIQUE KEY tabname .

  DATA: lt_obj_arch_runs TYPE TABLE OF ty_obj_arch_runs,
        ls_arch_runs     TYPE ty_arch_runs,
        lt_objects       TYPE ty_t_objects_for_tables,
        wa_objects       TYPE ty_s_objects_for_table,
        wa_objects_obj   TYPE ty_s_object,
        lt_tabnames      TYPE tttabname,
        archobj_wa       TYPE adk_ccms_object,
        archobj          TYPE adk_ccms_objects,
        nb_tables        TYPE i.
  FIELD-SYMBOLS:
    <objs> TYPE LINE OF ty_t_objects_for_tables,
    <obj>  TYPE ty_s_object.

  DATA: ls_archdef  TYPE ty_obj_arch_def,
        ls_archruns TYPE ty_obj_arch_runs.

  "Check archiving
  IF sy-dbsys(3) = 'HDB'.
    SORT gt_tables BY real_size DESCENDING.
  ELSE.
    SORT gt_tables BY est_size DESCENDING.
  ENDIF.
  CASE jobname.
    WHEN c_hrcjobname.
      nb_tables = 2000.
    WHEN OTHERS.
      nb_tables = 100.
  ENDCASE.
  LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> TO nb_tables.
    APPEND <item>-table_name TO lt_tabnames.
  ENDLOOP.
  TRY.
      CALL METHOD ('CL_ADK_CCMS_GET_OBJECTS')=>('GET_OBJECTS')
        EXPORTING
          it_tabnames            = lt_tabnames
          iv_delete_objects_only = abap_true
          iv_get_all_tables      = abap_false
        IMPORTING
          et_objects_for_tables  = lt_objects.
    CATCH cx_sy_dyn_call_illegal_class
          cx_sy_dyn_call_illegal_method
          cx_root.
      "read the minimum number of tables
      LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> TO nb_tables.
        CALL FUNCTION 'ADK_CCMS_GET_OBJECTS'
          EXPORTING
            table                      = <item>-db_table
            delete_objects_only        = 'X'
          TABLES
            objects                    = archobj
          EXCEPTIONS
            table_not_found            = 1
            pool_or_cluster_not_in_use = 2
            no_object_found            = 3
            table_is_not_transparent   = 4
            OTHERS                     = 5.
        IF sy-subrc IS NOT INITIAL.
          "ok no archiving information
        ENDIF.
        wa_objects-tabname = <item>-table_name.
        LOOP AT archobj INTO archobj_wa.
          wa_objects_obj-object = archobj_wa-object.
          MOVE archobj_wa-objtext TO wa_objects_obj-object_text.
          wa_objects_obj-sign = archobj_wa-sign.
          APPEND wa_objects_obj TO wa_objects-objects.
        ENDLOOP.
        IF wa_objects-objects[] IS NOT INITIAL.
          READ TABLE lt_objects WITH KEY tabname = wa_objects-tabname TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS BINARY SEARCH.
          INSERT wa_objects INTO lt_objects INDEX sy-tabix.
        ENDIF.
        CLEAR: wa_objects, wa_objects_obj.
      ENDLOOP.
  ENDTRY.
  CLEAR lt_tabnames[].

  "get 10 last archiving runs dates of each objects
  LOOP AT lt_objects ASSIGNING <objs>.
    ls_arch_runs-table_name = <objs>-tabname.
    LOOP AT <objs>-objects ASSIGNING <obj>.
      ls_archdef-object = <obj>-object.
      APPEND ls_archdef TO ls_arch_runs-objects.
      TRY.
          SELECT object creat_date AS arclrun FROM (c_admi_run) UP TO 10 ROWS INTO TABLE lt_obj_arch_runs
            WHERE object = <obj>-object AND status = 1
            ORDER BY creat_date DESCENDING.
          LOOP AT lt_obj_arch_runs INTO ls_archruns.
            APPEND ls_archruns TO ls_arch_runs-runs.
          ENDLOOP.
        CATCH cx_sy_dynamic_osql_semantics. "#EC NO_HANDLER
      ENDTRY.
    ENDLOOP.
    APPEND ls_arch_runs TO gt_arch_runs.
    CLEAR ls_arch_runs.
  ENDLOOP.
  LOOP AT gt_arch_runs INTO ls_arch_runs.
    SORT ls_arch_runs-runs BY arclrun DESCENDING.
    SORT ls_arch_runs-objects BY object.

    "below code is only relevant for ful mode
    READ TABLE gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WITH KEY table_name = ls_arch_runs-table_name BINARY SEARCH.
    IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
      IF sy-dbsys(3) = 'HDB'.
        real_elarch = real_elarch + <item>-real_size.
      ELSE.
        est_elarch = est_elarch + <item>-est_size.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.
  SORT gt_tables BY table_name.
ENDFORM.                    "get_dvm_info

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form get_topcs
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       estimate the size of the largest N partitions
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*

FORM get_topcs USING    sizefield TYPE fieldname
               CHANGING l_topcs   TYPE numeric.
  DATA three_parts   LIKE max_partition_rc.
  FIELD-SYMBOLS <fs> TYPE any.

  SORT gt_tables BY (sizefield) DESCENDING.
  CLEAR count.
  IF sy-dbsys(3) = 'HDB'.
    LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WHERE store = 'CS'.
      ADD 1 TO count.
      IF count > 3.
        EXIT.
      ENDIF.
      ASSIGN COMPONENT sizefield OF STRUCTURE <item> TO <fs>.
      IF <item>-part_id = 0. "cannot be 0 except cal mode.
        l_topcs = l_topcs + <fs>.
      ELSE.
        l_topcs = l_topcs + <fs> / <item>-part_id.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.
  ELSE.
    LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item> WHERE store = 'CS'.
      ADD 1 TO count.
      IF count > 3.
        EXIT.
      ENDIF.
      ASSIGN COMPONENT sizefield OF STRUCTURE <item> TO <fs>.
      three_parts = max_partition_rc * 3.
      IF <item>-record_count >= three_parts.
        IF l_topcs IS INITIAL.
          l_topcs = 3 * ( <fs> * max_partition_rc ) / <item>-record_count.
          EXIT. "if biggest table is partitioned then consider 3
          "partitions of this table as 3 largest objects.
        ELSE. "first table not partitioned but second is.
          l_topcs = l_topcs + 2 * ( <fs> * max_partition_rc ) / <item>-record_count.
        ENDIF.
      ELSE.
        l_topcs = l_topcs + <fs>.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    "get_topcs

AT SELECTION-SCREEN ON VALUE-REQUEST FOR p_guid.
  PERFORM call_f4_help USING 'P_GUID'.

AT SELECTION-SCREEN ON VALUE-REQUEST FOR p_guid_c.
  PERFORM call_f4_help USING 'P_GUID_C'.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form call_F4_help
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       Call F4 help for Sizing GUID
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM call_f4_help USING f4_param_name TYPE clike.

  TYPES:
    BEGIN OF ty_sizing, "replace this by dynamic using l_dfies
      sizing_guid       TYPE guid_16,
      crdate            TYPE sydats,
      crtime            TYPE sytime,
      report_version(6) TYPE c,
      nb_tables         TYPE int4,
      nb_errors         TYPE int4,
      total_sizing1     TYPE dec20,
    END OF ty_sizing.

  DATA: l_sizing_guids TYPE TABLE OF ty_sizing,
        l_dfies        TYPE TABLE OF dfies,
        l_alldfies     TYPE TABLE OF dfies,
        wa_dfies       TYPE dfies,
        offset         TYPE doffset.
  FIELD-SYMBOLS <sizing> TYPE ty_sizing.
  CONSTANTS c_sdf_hdbsizings TYPE tabname VALUE '/SDF/HDBSIZING'.

  CALL FUNCTION 'DDIF_FIELDINFO_GET'
    EXPORTING
      tabname        = c_sdf_hdbsizings
    TABLES
      dfies_tab      = l_alldfies
    EXCEPTIONS
      not_found      = 1
      internal_error = 2
      OTHERS         = 3.
  IF sy-subrc IS NOT INITIAL.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  LOOP AT l_alldfies INTO wa_dfies.
    CASE wa_dfies-fieldname.
      WHEN 'SIZING_GUID'.
        wa_dfies-reptext   = 'Sizing GUID'.                 "#EC NOTEXT
      WHEN 'CRDATE'.
        wa_dfies-scrtext_s = 'Exec. date'.                  "#EC NOTEXT
      WHEN 'CRTIME'.
        wa_dfies-scrtext_s = 'Exec. time'.                  "#EC NOTEXT
      WHEN 'TOTAL_SIZING1'.
        wa_dfies-reptext = 'Memory sizing in MB'.           "#EC NOTEXT
      WHEN OTHERS.
    ENDCASE.
    IF   wa_dfies-fieldname = 'SIZING_GUID'
      OR wa_dfies-fieldname = 'CRDATE'
      OR wa_dfies-fieldname = 'CRTIME'
      OR wa_dfies-fieldname = 'REPORT_VERSION'
      OR wa_dfies-fieldname = 'NB_TABLES'
      OR wa_dfies-fieldname = 'NB_ERRORS'
      OR wa_dfies-fieldname = 'TOTAL_SIZING1'.
      wa_dfies-offset = offset.
      ADD wa_dfies-intlen TO offset.
      APPEND wa_dfies TO l_dfies.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.

  SELECT sizing_guid crdate crtime report_version nb_tables nb_errors total_sizing1 FROM (c_sdf_hdbsizings)
    INTO CORRESPONDING FIELDS OF TABLE l_sizing_guids
    WHERE report_name = sy-repid OR report_name = c_hrcjobname.

  LOOP AT l_sizing_guids ASSIGNING <sizing>.
    <sizing>-total_sizing1 = <sizing>-total_sizing1 / 1024 / 1024.
  ENDLOOP.
  SORT l_sizing_guids BY crdate DESCENDING crtime DESCENDING.

  CALL FUNCTION 'F4IF_INT_TABLE_VALUE_REQUEST'
    EXPORTING
      retfield        = 'SIZING_GUID'
      dynpprog        = sy-repid
      dynpnr          = sy-dynnr
      dynprofield     = f4_param_name
      window_title    = 'Sizing results available'      "#EC NOTEXT
      value_org       = 'S'
    TABLES
      value_tab       = l_sizing_guids
      field_tab       = l_dfies
    EXCEPTIONS
      parameter_error = 1
      no_values_found = 2
      OTHERS          = 3.
  IF sy-subrc IS NOT INITIAL.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form b2gb_subtotals
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*        Convert all variables to GiB
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM b2gb_subtotals.

  LOOP AT gt_tables ASSIGNING <item>.
    b2gb <item>-est_size.
    b2gb <item>-est_hl_size.
    b2gb <item>-est_paged_size.
    b2gb <item>-est_disk_size.
    b2gb <item>-est_pk_size.
    b2gb <item>-est_nuk_size.

    b2gb <item>-real_size.
    b2gb <item>-real_hl_size.
    b2gb <item>-real_paged_size.
    b2gb <item>-real_disk_size.
    b2gb <item>-real_pk_size.
    b2gb <item>-real_nuk_size.

    b2gb <item>-source_size.
    b2gb <item>-opt_size.
    b2gb <item>-opt_pageable_size.
    b2gb <item>-real_jec_size.
    b2gb <item>-real_esh_size.
  ENDLOOP.
  LOOP AT gt_sfin2 ASSIGNING <sfin>.
    b2gb <sfin>-size.
    b2gb <sfin>-ssize.
    b2gb <sfin>-osize.
  ENDLOOP.
  LOOP AT gt_ec_pca ASSIGNING <ec_pca>.
    b2gb <ec_pca>-size.
    b2gb <ec_pca>-ssize.
    b2gb <ec_pca>-osize.
  ENDLOOP.
  LOOP AT gt_aging ASSIGNING <aging>.
    b2gb <aging>-hist_size.
    b2gb <aging>-size.
  ENDLOOP.
  LOOP AT gt_slog ASSIGNING <slog>.
    b2gb <slog>-size.
    b2gb <slog>-ssize.
    b2gb <slog>-osize.
  ENDLOOP.
  LOOP AT gt_inplace ASSIGNING <upgrade>.
    b2gb <upgrade>-size.
    b2gb <upgrade>-pksize.
    b2gb <upgrade>-disksize.
  ENDLOOP.
  LOOP AT gt_shadow ASSIGNING <upgrade>.
    b2gb <upgrade>-size.
    b2gb <upgrade>-pksize.
    b2gb <upgrade>-disksize.
  ENDLOOP.
  LOOP AT gt_sogrp ASSIGNING <sogrp>.
    b2gb <sogrp>-size.
    b2gb <sogrp>-opt_size.
  ENDLOOP.
  LOOP AT gt_ml ASSIGNING <ml>.
    b2gb <ml>-size.
    b2gb <ml>-ssize.
    b2gb <ml>-osize.
  ENDLOOP.
  LOOP AT gt_soh2s4 ASSIGNING <soh2s4>.
    b2gb <soh2s4>-soh_size.
    b2gb <soh2s4>-opt_size.
    b2gb <soh2s4>-opt_hl_size.
  ENDLOOP.

  b2gb diskadmin.
  b2gb codestack.
  "details - real
  b2gb cs_col.
  b2gb cs_pk.
  b2gb cs_rid.
  b2gb cs_udiv.
  b2gb cs_uk.
  b2gb cs_nuk.
  b2gb cs_jec.
  b2gb cs_aging.
  b2gb cs_ft.
  b2gb cs_hcard.
  b2gb cs_mcard.
  b2gb cs_lcard.
  b2gb cs_ucard.
  b2gb rs_col.
  b2gb rs_pk.
  b2gb rs_sk.
  b2gb cshl.
  b2gb rshl.
  b2gb cs_mlob.
  b2gb rs_mlob.
  b2gb cs_k.
  b2gb cs_total.
  b2gb rs_total.
  b2gb init_data.
  b2gb init_ws.
  b2gb hl.
  b2gb hlch.
  b2gb twocs.
  b2gb initdisk.
  b2gb init_size.
  b2gb opt_data.
  b2gb opt_size.
  b2gb optdisk.
  b2gb opt_ws.

  "details - est.
  b2gb est_cs_col.
  b2gb est_cs_pk.
  b2gb est_cs_rid.
  b2gb est_cs_udiv.
  b2gb est_cs_uk.
  b2gb est_cs_nuk.
  b2gb est_cs_hcard.
  b2gb est_cs_mcard.
  b2gb est_cs_lcard.
  b2gb est_cs_ucard.
  b2gb est_rs_col.
  b2gb est_rs_pk.
  b2gb est_rs_sk.
  b2gb est_cshl.
  b2gb est_rshl.
  b2gb est_rs_mlob.
  b2gb est_rs_mlob.
  b2gb est_cs_k.
  b2gb est_cs_total.
  b2gb est_rs_total.
  b2gb est_init_data.
  b2gb est_init_ws.
  b2gb est_hl.

  b2gb est_sfin_inv.
  b2gb est_twocs.

  "Finance
  b2gb est_sfintab.
